Program Specialist (Contract Developer Training Program)BackShareSubmit your resume
Would you like to become a Certified Texas Contract Developer? Are ready to make a career change? Do you have a background in sales, customer service, and/or marketing?  If so this assignment could be for you!  In this role you will work with a fantastic contract administration and procurement team and be trained to become a certified Texas Contract Developer.

 


The Team You Will Be Joining

This state agency serves as the chief steward of the State of Texas’ finances. In this capacity, the agency works with Texans through vital roles: tax collector, chief accountant, chief revenue estimator, and chief treasurer.
 

Major Duties

Works with senior staff to complete procurements and manage contracts
Collects information and performs product research for program agency needs.  
Provides analysis and quality control for agency procurements.
Markets program(s) to internal and external groups to improve communication, capture pain points and lessons learned.
Collects, organizes, analyzes, and/or prepares materials in response to request for program information and reports.
Collaborates with program staff in determining trends and resolving technical problems for contract and procurement data.
Performs special projects and other related duties as assigned
 

What We’re Looking For

Experience in client relationship/customer service, sales, marketing, and management related functions. 
Experience working within a team structure and providing customer service or exercising positive customer relations throughout an organization. 
Experience with scheduling meetings, leading meetings, and the creation and monitoring of project schedules. 
Experience working developing documents and assembling with large amounts of data or documents using Word, Excel or and other other business related tools (e.g., Salesforce, PowerPoint, Visio, Microsoft SharePoint, etc.). 
Certification as a Certified Texas Contract Developer (CTCD) must be obtained within 3 months of employment

 

Exciting Opportunity Details

Rate: $32.00 per hour
Length of Engagement: 6 months; possibility of full time placement 
Days/Hours: Monday - Friday; Standard business hours (40 hours/week)
Location: Austin, TX 78701
 

The Peak Performers Difference

Comprehensive medical, dental, and vision insurance coverage available from the first day of the month following 60 days of employment.
Participation in a 403(b)-retirement plan.
Priority placement for qualified applicants with chronic medical conditions and/or disabilities.
Weekly payments through direct deposit.
In business since 1994 and thousands of job placements.

---

**ASSISTANT**:
**Job Summary:**

The role of Program Specialist (Contract Developer Training Program) involves training to become a Certified Texas Contract Developer. The candidate will work with a contract administration and procurement team within a state agency responsible for managing Texas&#x27; finances, including roles such as tax collector, chief accountant, chief revenue estimator, and chief treasurer. Major duties include working with senior staff to manage procurements and contracts, conducting product research, performing analysis and quality control, marketing the program, responding to information requests, collaborating on technical problem-solving, and executing special projects. The role requires experience in sales, customer service, marketing, and management, with skills in team collaboration, customer relations, meeting management, and document handling using business tools like Word, Excel, and Salesforce.

**Relating to Your History:**

Given your diverse background spanning the military, technology, sales, and arboriculture, you bring a unique blend of disciplined project management, technical expertise, and customer relationship skills that align well with this role. Your experience in sales and marketing directly translates to the client relationship and program marketing aspects of the job. Your work in arboriculture and consulting demonstrates your ability to conduct detailed research, analysis, and quality control, which are crucial for procurement tasks. Additionally, your passion for leveraging technology for ecological restoration shows a strong capacity for handling complex data and utilizing business tools, making you well-suited for the document and data management responsibilities.

**Assessment of Likeness to Do This Job:**

You are highly likely to excel in this position due to:

1. **Sales and Marketing Experience:** Your background in sales and customer service aligns with the job’s need for client relationship management and program marketing.
2. **Technical and Analytical Skills:** Your involvement in technology and soil science showcases your ability to conduct research, analyze data, and provide quality control.
3. **Project Management:** Your military discipline and consulting roles highlight your capability to manage projects, lead meetings, and work within a team structure.
4. **Software Proficiency:** Your familiarity with business tools such as Excel and project management software positions you well for handling the document assembly and data management tasks.

Overall, your multifaceted experience, combined with your passion for ecological and technological integration, positions you as a strong candidate for this role.

Dear Hiring Team,

I am excited to apply for the Commercial Sales Arborist position with SavATree. With a diverse background that spans arboriculture, environmental science, and high-security IT management, I am uniquely positioned to bring a blend of technical expertise, problem-solving skills, and a passion for tree care to this role.

In my current role as the Founder of Soil Grower, I have successfully launched a startup focused on soil health technologies, leveraging AI, remote sensing, and satellite imagery. This experience has sharpened my project management skills, honed my data analysis capabilities, and reinforced my commitment to environmental stewardship. My work has involved extensive collaboration with partners, strategic planning, and the application of cutting-edge technologies to improve soil and plant health, directly aligning with SavATree&#x27;s mission to preserve and care for trees and plants.

During my tenure as a Contract Arborist with Tree Mann Solutions, I conducted comprehensive tree surveys and assessments, managed data collection for over 8,000 trees, and provided Plant Health Care (PHC) services. I utilized GIS and remote sensing tools to map and analyze ecological data, enhancing project accuracy and operational efficiency. This hands-on experience in arboriculture and environmental management has equipped me with the skills necessary to diagnose and monitor landscapes effectively, estimate jobs, and ensure the health and well-being of clients&#x27; landscapes.

As a Climbing Arborist with Davey Tree Experts, I conducted health assessments, precision pruning, and safe tree removals, all while upholding the highest standards of environmental sustainability and safety. My work in urban forestry practices to enhance ecological resilience and my focus on the holistic care and treatment of trees are directly relevant to the responsibilities of a Commercial Sales Arborist at SavATree.

My background in IT, particularly as a Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army, has instilled in me a strong attention to detail, technical proficiency, and the ability to manage complex projects under pressure. These skills, combined with my experience in customer service and training, will enable me to effectively communicate with clients, diagnose their needs, and provide industry-leading solutions for their tree, plant, and lawn care health.

I am particularly drawn to this role because of the opportunity to work closely with field specialists, develop and support a sales territory, and make a positive impact on the environment every day. SavATree&#x27;s commitment to preserving trees and plants aligns perfectly with my personal mission to enhance environmental sustainability through innovative solutions.

I am enthusiastic about the possibility of bringing my unique blend of skills and experiences to SavATree. I am committed to providing exceptional service, developing new business, and ensuring the health and safety of the landscapes we serve together. Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to discuss how my background, skills, and passion align with the goals of SavATree.

Warmest regards,

George Steward

Leading IT services for over 800 personnel in high-pressure environments has instilled in me a meticulous attention to detail and a robust problem-solving mindset. These skills will enable me to excel in managing contracts, performing product research, and providing analysis and quality control.

Your agency&#x27;s commitment to serving Texans through vital financial roles resonates with my personal mission to contribute positively to my community and environment.

I look forward to discussing how my background, skills, and passion align with the goals of your agency.

job description:
The Biomimicry Institute is a fully remote organization.  However, preferred candidates are from the states of California, Washington, Montana, New York or Pennsylvania.  

Applicants from states with salary band posting requirements:  Salary is determined based on internal equity; internal salary ranges; market data/ranges; applicant’s skills; prior relevant experience; degrees or certifications, etc. The salary for this position ranges from $90,000 - $110,000.

**We encourage people of all backgrounds and experiences to apply. Even if you don’t think you are a perfect fit, apply anyway - you might have qualifications we haven’t even thought of yet.**

Job Purpose
The Director of Strategic Communications is responsible for elevating the Institute’s profile and influence through strategic communication, media relations, and brand management. This individual will develop and execute comprehensive communication strategies to amplify the Institute’s mission, managing a team of communication professionals, and overseeing the integration of innovative public relations techniques to engage new audiences and support organizational growth. The Director of Strategic Communications will develop strategic plans for the institute’s communication and amplification objectives, collaborate with leadership on evolving program and brand strategy, and oversee the expansion of the Institute’s presence across social media and global stages.

Essential Functions
Strategic Communications:
In collaboration with the CEO and program leads, develop and implement a comprehensive communications and external affairs strategy, including defining short- and long-term goals and objectives to advance the Institute’s mission and broaden awareness of its programs, focusing on both stakeholder audiences as well as untapped potential audiences.  
Collaborate with CEO and program Directors to refine and evolve the Institute’s brand strategy and messaging framework.
Spearhead strategic initiatives to identify and engage untapped audiences, leveraging data-driven insights and innovative approaches.
Working with the Director of Development, create and execute amplification campaigns, donor engagement strategies, and public events through the engagement of external partners and consultants
Seek out revenue generating opportunities specific to communications (i.e. webinars, sponsored film spots, etc.)
Organize and promote high-profile PR events and manage the editorial calendar for the planning and timely execution of all communications activities.
Ensure cross-collaboration between communications and other departments and ensure that adequate support from communications is provided for priority projects and/or campaigns.
Collaborate with leadership to promote positive internal communications that keep all staff members up-to-date and promote an integrated and collaborative environment.
25% of this role will be focused on the Design for Transformation program to deliver a comprehensive global narrative and storytelling program, working with external agencies, global partners and funders.
Public Relations:
Champion the Institute’s brand, ensuring a strong and consistent presence both internally and externally.
Manage the Institute’s social media strategy, driving audience growth and engagement, with a focus on increasing distribution channels and media contacts.
Ensure consistency and impact in messaging across all digital content platforms.
Lead media relations efforts, serving as the primary contact for media inquiries and managing publicity campaigns.
Develop, update, and manage inventory of internal and external communications tools and platforms across organization.
Management:
Develop and manage a communications budget, including forecasting requirements; coordinate creative services for communications materials; hire and support contractors, including managing work plans, providing feedback, and leading meetings.
Oversee the production of key communication assets, including annual reports, development collateral, digital content, and media materials.
Manage direct reports by:
Participate in the recruitment, selection and onboarding of new Communications employees.
Look for ways to streamline communications operations and enhance team productivity.
Communicating and setting clear job expectations
Continually evaluate performance, culminating in an annual written performance evaluation. 
Lead, mentor and support professional development of team.
Assess team skills and provide training plans for skill/growth development.
Creation of RPF’s for independent contractor services.
Establish clear work order guidelines for marketing and PR consultants.
Establish clear work order guidelines for contractors.
Ensure completion of all stated objectives prior to invoice approval.
QUALIFICATIONS
Education and Experience
BA in a related field and 10+ years of combined experience in communications, marketing and/or public relations. 
Experience in brand management, media relations, and digital amplification of mission based programs a plus.
Experience synthesizing and disseminating information through multiple distribution channels.
Excellent working knowledge of the social media landscape, with an understanding of community activation and engagement.
Excellent knowledge of biomimicry. If not trained in biomimicry, then must complete advanced training.
Proven commitment to diversity, equity, and inclusion:
Ability to actively cultivate and develop inclusive and equitable working relationships with coworkers, management, board members and clients.
Employs anti-racist practices and principles to accomplish work.
Experience working directly with people from diverse racial, ethnic, and socioeconomic backgrounds.
Incorporates an anti-racist and anti-oppressive lens into TBI programs.
Teaches using equitable and inclusive pedagogy.
Skills/Abilities
Personal qualities of integrity, credibility, and dedication to the mission of the Biomimicry Institute.
A successful track record in setting priorities; keen analytic, organization and problem solving skills which support and enable sound decision making. Keeps track of responsibilities and meets deadlines and goals.
Adaptable—manages a constantly changing remote work environment; learns to collaborate with geographically dispersed new team members, etc.
Clear, direct, and succinct writer. Strong editing skills, including an ability to write for a variety of audiences and channels.
An eye for design, enough to effectively communicate vision.
Comfortable learning and using the digital tools the Biomimicry Institute uses—with little to no assistance, and willing to try out new technologies and work tools.
Self-sufficient—takes the initiative and completes work without undue supervision
Strong communication and relationship building skills. Ensures every team member is given a chance to speak. Demonstrates the ability to understand others’ thoughts and feelings (social sensitivity). Respectfully engages in disagreements. Keeps team members informed/updated. Is a good active listener who understands what’s being asked of them and the priorities of various tasks.
Physical Requirements
The physical demands described here are representative of that which an employee encounters while performing the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodation can be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.
Activities that occur constantly are communicating effectively with others to exchange information; assessing the accuracy, neatness and thoroughness of the work; repeating motions efficiently that may include the wrists, hands and/or fingers; prolonged periods of working at a computer; remaining in a stationary position, often standing or sitting for prolonged periods.
Activities that occur occasionally are moving about to accomplish tasks or moving from one worksite to another; adjusting or moving objects less than 50 pounds in all directions.
Work Environment (Remote)
The work environment described here is representative of that which an employee encounters while performing the essential functions of this job. Reasonable accommodation can be made to enable individuals with disabilities to perform the essential functions.
Duties are performed in a home workspace. Employees are expected to maintain their home workspace in a safe manner, free from safety hazards.
Flexibility to respond to various global time zones.
May require up to 10-20% travel.

### Step 3: Craft Your Strategic Plan

#### **How did you learn about The Biomimicry Institute?**

My journey with The Biomimicry Institute began many years ago when I first stumbled upon the concept of biomimicry. The idea of drawing inspiration from nature to solve human challenges resonated deeply with me. Over the past five years, I have dedicated myself to understanding nature not just as an observer but as a participant. This journey has been profoundly influenced by my late discovery of being autistic, which I now see as a superpower that enhances my ability to understand and connect with the natural world.

I have followed The Biomimicry Institute&#x27;s progress and growth with great admiration, dreaming of one day contributing to its mission. My work in environmental science, arboriculture, and strategic communications has been driven by a desire to make our society function better for the environment. I have developed a deep understanding of the interconnectedness of ecosystems and the importance of sustainable practices.

#### **Strategic Plan for Elevating The Biomimicry Institute**

**Vision:**
To amplify The Biomimicry Institute’s mission by leveraging innovative communication strategies and expanding its presence across diverse platforms and audiences.

**Goals:**
1. **Increase Global Awareness:**
   - Develop and implement a comprehensive global narrative and storytelling program.
   - Engage with global partners and funders to amplify the Institute’s mission.

2. **Enhance Brand Visibility:**
   - Refine and evolve the Institute’s brand strategy and messaging framework.
   - Spearhead strategic initiatives to identify and engage untapped audiences.

3. **Strengthen Media Relations:**
   - Lead media relations efforts, serving as the primary contact for media inquiries.
   - Manage publicity campaigns and increase distribution channels and media contacts.

4. **Boost Digital Engagement:**
   - Oversee the Institute’s social media strategy, driving audience growth and engagement.
   - Ensure consistency and impact in messaging across all digital content platforms.

5. **Promote Internal Collaboration:**
   - Foster positive internal communications to promote an integrated and collaborative environment.
   - Ensure cross-collaboration between communications and other departments.

**Action Plan:**

**Short-term (0-6 months):**
- Conduct a comprehensive audit of current communication strategies and tools.
- Develop a refined brand strategy and messaging framework in collaboration with leadership.
- Launch initial strategic initiatives to engage untapped audiences.
- Organize high-profile PR events to boost immediate visibility.

**Medium-term (6-12 months):**
- Implement a global narrative and storytelling program.
- Expand the Institute’s presence across social media and global stages.
- Develop and execute amplification campaigns in collaboration with external partners.

**Long-term (12+ months):**
- Continuously evaluate and adapt communication strategies based on data-driven insights.
- Seek out and capitalize on revenue-generating opportunities specific to communications.
- Establish The Biomimicry Institute as a leading voice in biomimicry and sustainability.

### Strategic Plan for Elevating The Biomimicry Institute

#### **How did you learn about The Biomimicry Institute?**

My journey with The Biomimicry Institute began many years ago when I first stumbled upon the concept of biomimicry. The idea of drawing inspiration from nature to solve human challenges resonated deeply with me. Over the past five years, I have dedicated myself to understanding nature not just as an observer but as a participant. This journey has been profoundly influenced by my late discovery of being autistic, which I now see as a superpower that enhances my ability to understand and connect with the natural world.

I have followed The Biomimicry Institute&#x27;s progress and growth with great admiration, dreaming of one day contributing to its mission. My work in environmental science, arboriculture, and strategic communications has been driven by a desire to make our society function better for the environment. I have developed a deep understanding of the interconnectedness of ecosystems and the importance of sustainable practices.

#### **Strategic Plan for Elevating The Biomimicry Institute**

**Vision:**
To amplify The Biomimicry Institute’s mission by leveraging innovative communication strategies and expanding its presence across diverse platforms and audiences.

**Goals:**
1. **Increase Global Awareness:**
   - Develop and implement a comprehensive global narrative and storytelling program.
   - Engage with global partners and funders to amplify the Institute’s mission.

2. **Enhance Brand Visibility:**
   - Refine and evolve the Institute’s brand strategy and messaging framework.
   - Spearhead strategic initiatives to identify and engage untapped audiences.

3. **Strengthen Media Relations:**
   - Lead media relations efforts, serving as the primary contact for media inquiries.
   - Manage publicity campaigns and increase distribution channels and media contacts.

4. **Boost Digital Engagement:**
   - Oversee the Institute’s social media strategy, driving audience growth and engagement.
   - Ensure consistency and impact in messaging across all digital content platforms.

5. **Promote Internal Collaboration:**
   - Foster positive internal communications to promote an integrated and collaborative environment.
   - Ensure cross-collaboration between communications and other departments.

**Action Plan:**

**Short-term (0-6 months):**
- Conduct a comprehensive audit of current communication strategies and tools.
- Develop a refined brand strategy and messaging framework in collaboration with leadership.
- Launch initial strategic initiatives to engage untapped audiences.
- Organize high-profile PR events to boost immediate visibility.

**Medium-term (6-12 months):**
- Implement a global narrative and storytelling program.
- Expand the Institute’s presence across social media and global stages.
- Develop and execute amplification campaigns in collaboration with external partners.

**Long-term (12+ months):**
- Continuously evaluate and adapt communication strategies based on data-driven insights.
- Seek out and capitalize on revenue-generating opportunities specific to communications.
- Establish The Biomimicry Institute as a leading voice in biomimicry and sustainability.

Dear Hiring Team,

I am thrilled to apply for the Director of Strategic Communications position at The Biomimicry Institute. This role perfectly aligns with my passion for nature-inspired solutions and my professional journey in strategic communications, brand management, and environmental science. My diverse experiences, including my unique perspective as an autistic individual, equip me with innovative thinking and a profound understanding of nature.

Over the past five years, I have been on a journey to understand nature by becoming an integral part of it. As the Founder of Soil Grower, I have combined AI, remote sensing, and satellite imagery to revolutionize soil health technologies. This role has honed my project management skills and strategic planning abilities, and most importantly, it has deepened my commitment to sustainability. My long-term strategy includes implementing Earth Power Lodge (EPL) systems to mimic natural processes, producing biochar and refining algae to accelerate ecological regeneration.

My work as a Contract Arborist with Tree Mann Solutions and as a Marketing and Outreach Specialist with REGENiTECH has equipped me with extensive experience in data collection, analysis, and strategic communication. I have successfully increased brand visibility and customer engagement, aligning with the goals of elevating The Biomimicry Institute’s profile.

My tenure as a Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army and as a Solutions Consultant at ServiceNow demonstrates my ability to manage high-stakes projects and lead teams effectively. These roles have also sharpened my problem-solving skills and attention to detail, which are crucial for managing comprehensive communication strategies.

I am particularly drawn to The Biomimicry Institute because of its mission to promote nature-inspired solutions for a sustainable world. As someone who identifies with the smilax plant—an autistic pioneer in ecosystem establishment—I bring a unique perspective to understanding and communicating the intricacies of nature. My journey with autism has become a superpower, allowing me to see connections in nature that others might overlook.

I am eager to bring my skills and passion to The Biomimicry Institute, where I can contribute to developing and executing comprehensive communication strategies, managing media relations, and amplifying the Institute’s mission on global stages. I am committed to achieving excellence in this role and advancing the Institute’s mission of biomimicry.

Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to discuss how my background, skills, and passion align with the goals of The Biomimicry Institute.

George Steward

**ASSISTANT**:
### Powerful Statement about the Exclusivity of Being a Technical Warrant Officer

Being a Technical Warrant Officer in the U.S. Army, specifically as a 255AP in the 7th Special Forces Group, represents an elite and highly specialized role. As a Technical Warrant Officer, I was one of the select few entrusted with high-level technical advisory responsibilities for the executive command team. This position demands unparalleled technical expertise, leadership, and the ability to operate under extreme pressure, making it a distinguished and highly respected role in the military and beyond.

---

### Email to Michael

**Subject: Recommendation for Executive Director of Technology Position at Liberty Hill ISD**

Hi Michael,

I hope this message finds you well. I&#x27;m reaching out to share an exciting opportunity and to ask for your support.

I recently applied for the Executive Director of Technology position at Liberty Hill ISD. With over 14 years of experience in IT management, strategic planning, and technology implementation, both in military and civilian sectors, I am confident in my ability to drive technological advancements and support the district&#x27;s educational mission.

As a former Technical Warrant Officer (255AP) in the 7th Special Forces Group, I served as a high-level technical advisor, managing complex projects that involved data migrations, network security, and infrastructure implementation. My experience has equipped me with the skills necessary to excel in this role and contribute positively to our community.

Given your connection with the school district, I would be incredibly grateful if you could speak to my abilities and potential contributions. Attached are my resume and cover letter for your reference.

Thank you for your support, and please let me know if there&#x27;s any additional information I can provide.

Best regards,

George Steward  
(737) 234-0110  
george@soilgrower.org

---

This email, along with the statement about your exclusive role as a Technical Warrant Officer, should provide Michael with the context and confidence to advocate effectively on your behalf. If you need any further adjustments or additional details, feel free to let me know!

**USER**:
refer back to my cover letter for the director of technology role to answer the following question. 

Describe how you would have a positive impact on student learning in this position.

I want to express the full extent of the value of learning to me as it has been my whole life. I am a first-principles learner who relies heavily on instinctual knowledge and I seek to make connections from abstract and often unrelated areas and ideas. My most important life goal is to expand and extend the level of knowledge and consciousness of mankind. I have sought to learn a vast array of information from many fields of study with the ultimate goal of understanding the universe from the smallest of microorganisms to the largest parts of the cosmos. We owe it to the younger generations to give it our all when teaching them how to thrive in this world.

How the heck do I say this without sounding like a crazy person?

How do I also add in my larger dreams and aspirations of building an Earth Power Lodge for the purpose of teaching young folks about closed-loop power generation systems and the byproducts of which help to regenerate soil. How this idea of growing soil is an expression of using the freedoms that we enjoy to maximize our efforts toward stopping the erosion of our civilization and accelerating the continuation of life.

---

**ASSISTANT**:
### Response for &quot;Describe how you would have a positive impact on student learning in this position.&quot;

As someone who deeply values learning and has pursued a wide range of knowledge across various fields, I bring a unique and holistic approach to education and technology. My life&#x27;s journey has been driven by a desire to understand the universe from the smallest microorganisms to the largest cosmic structures. This curiosity and dedication to expanding human knowledge are qualities I strive to instill in the next generation.

In the role of Executive Director of Technology, my impact on student learning would be multifaceted:

1. **Holistic Learning Approach:** I am a first-principles learner who relies on instinctual knowledge and makes connections between abstract and seemingly unrelated ideas. This approach encourages students to think critically and innovatively, fostering a deeper understanding of complex concepts.

2. **Expanding Knowledge and Consciousness:** My ultimate goal is to expand and extend the level of knowledge and consciousness of mankind. By integrating advanced technology and fostering a culture of curiosity, I aim to inspire students to explore, question, and learn continuously. This can be achieved through creating interactive and engaging learning environments that utilize the latest technological advancements.

3. **Building Earth Power Lodge:** I envision building an Earth Power Lodge as a hub for teaching students about closed-loop power generation systems and their positive impact on the environment. This initiative would provide hands-on learning experiences in sustainable practices, showing students how technology can be harnessed to regenerate soil and support ecological balance.

4. **Maximizing Educational Impact:** Using the freedoms we enjoy, we have the responsibility to maximize our efforts toward stopping the erosion of our civilization and accelerating the continuation of life. in a texas school district they are asking this question on a job application. they say for life, but what are the actual legal stipulations on how far back to report information?

Have you ever been convicted of, plead guilty or no contest to, or received probation, suspension, or deferred adjudication for a misdemeanor or felony involving any criminal offenses in your lifetime including, but not limited to, drug or alcohol-related offenses, family violence, driving offenses, dishonesty, fraud, deceit, theft, misrepresentation, deliberate violence, offense of a sexual nature, or acts constituting abuse under the Texas Family code, other Texas statutes, and/or any out of state or federal agencies?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
In Texas, school districts require applicants to disclose any criminal history involving convictions, guilty pleas, no contest pleas, probation, suspension, or deferred adjudication for misdemeanors or felonies. This includes a wide range of offenses such as drug or alcohol-related offenses, family violence, driving offenses, dishonesty, fraud, deceit, theft, misrepresentation, deliberate violence, offenses of a sexual nature, or acts constituting abuse.

### Legal Stipulations for Reporting Criminal History

**1. Reporting Time Frame:**
   - **Lifetime Disclosure:** Texas school districts generally require applicants to disclose any relevant criminal history over their entire lifetime. There is no legal limitation on how far back you must report this information.

**2. Types of Offenses:**
   - **Misdemeanors and Felonies:** Both types must be reported.
   - **Specific Offenses:** Includes drug or alcohol-related offenses, family violence, driving offenses, dishonesty, fraud, deceit, theft, misrepresentation, deliberate violence, offenses of a sexual nature, or acts constituting abuse under Texas Family Code and other statutes, including out-of-state or federal offenses.

**3. Types of Legal Outcomes:**
   - **Convictions:** Must be disclosed.
   - **Guilty or No Contest Pleas:** Must be disclosed.
   - **Probation:** Must be disclosed.
   - **Suspension:** Must be disclosed.
   - **Deferred Adjudication:** Must be disclosed.

**4. Exceptions and Considerations:**
   - **Expunged or Sealed Records:** If a record has been legally expunged or sealed, it may not need to be disclosed. However, this depends on the specifics of the expungement order and the context in which the question is asked.
   - **Juvenile Records:** Juvenile records are often treated differently, but it is advisable to consult with legal counsel regarding disclosure requirements.

### Importance of Disclosure

Failure to fully disclose required information can have serious consequences, including withdrawal of job offers or termination of employment if the information is later discovered. Transparency and honesty in reporting are crucial.

### Recommendations:

1. **Review Your Records:** Obtain a copy of your criminal record to ensure you accurately report any required information.
2. **Consult Legal Counsel:** If you are unsure about your obligations or if specific records need to be disclosed, consult with an attorney specializing in employment or criminal law in Texas.
3. **Be Honest:** Complete the application thoroughly and truthfully, disclosing all relevant information as required by the school district.

By following these guidelines, you can ensure compliance with the legal requirements for disclosing criminal history in your job application for a Texas school district.

**ASSISTANT**:
### Expert Assessment of the Technology Controls Associate - Cybersecurity Role at Real

**Role Overview:**
The Technology Controls Associate in Cybersecurity at Real is responsible for managing technology platform assessments, ensuring readiness and remediation, and performing IT general and application controls testing. This includes assessing and documenting control processes, tracking program progress, and ensuring adherence to security standards. The role demands a strong understanding of IT controls, cloud technologies, and cybersecurity practices.

**Key Duties:**
1. **Control Testing:** Perform IT general and application control testing to ensure systems comply with security and regulatory standards.
2. **Platform Evaluation:** Evaluate new and existing technology platforms to ensure they meet control and security standards.
3. **Remediation:** Identify and address security vulnerabilities, ensuring timely remediation.
4. **Documentation:** Maintain high-quality program documentation and communicate progress to senior management.
5. **Stakeholder Collaboration:** Work with internal and external stakeholders to understand and improve control processes.

**Setting Yourself Apart:**
1. **Leverage Military Experience:** Highlight your experience managing high-security systems and implementing rigorous security measures in the military. Emphasize the unique challenges and high-stakes environments you have navigated.
2. **Focus on Security Projects:** Detail specific cybersecurity projects and initiatives you led at ServiceNow and other roles. Mention any relevant security assessments, audits, or control implementations.
3. **Certifications:** Ensure your certifications (CompTIA Security+, ITIL Foundations, etc.) are prominently displayed, showing your commitment to staying current in the field.
4. **Results-Oriented:** Provide concrete examples of how your interventions led to improved security postures or compliance within your previous roles.
5. **Cross-Functional Skills:** Emphasize your ability to work across different teams and stakeholders, a crucial skill for ensuring comprehensive security controls.

### Impact on Real Estate and Connection to Soil Grower

**Impact on Real Estate:**
As a Technology Controls Associate, you would contribute to ensuring secure, seamless real estate transactions. By safeguarding the technology platforms that power Real&#x27;s services, you ensure that agents and customers can trust the system, leading to smoother transactions and a better overall experience.

**Connection to Soil Grower:**
Being a soil grower is about nurturing and building resilient foundations. In real estate, this translates to creating a secure, trustworthy platform where people can confidently acquire property. Just as healthy soil is fundamental to a thriving ecosystem, robust cybersecurity is essential for a thriving real estate environment. Your role in securing Real&#x27;s technology would enable individuals to build their dreams on a foundation they can trust, echoing the principles of growth, resilience, and sustainability that underpin your work with Soil Grower.

1. **Holistic Learning Approach:** I am a first-principles learner who relies on instinctual knowledge and makes connections between abstract and seemingly unrelated ideas. This approach encourages students to think critically and innovatively, fostering a deeper understanding of complex concepts.

2. **Expanding Knowledge and Consciousness:** My ultimate goal is to expand and extend the level of knowledge and consciousness of mankind. By integrating advanced technology and fostering a culture of curiosity, I aim to inspire students to explore, question, and learn continuously. This can be achieved through creating interactive and engaging learning environments that utilize the latest technological advancements.

3. **Building Earth Power Lodge:** I envision building an Earth Power Lodge as a hub for teaching students about closed-loop power generation systems and their positive impact on the environment. This initiative would provide hands-on learning experiences in sustainable practices, showing students how technology can be harnessed to regenerate soil and support ecological balance.

4. **Maximizing Educational Impact:** Using the freedoms we enjoy, we have the responsibility to maximize our efforts toward stopping the erosion of our civilization and accelerating the continuation of life. By integrating my extensive IT experience and my passion for sustainable technology, I will ensure that students are not only technologically proficient but also environmentally conscious and prepared to tackle future challenges.

5. **Fostering Curiosity and Innovation:** My experience has taught me the importance of fostering a culture of curiosity and innovation. As Executive Director of Technology, I will create opportunities for students to engage with technology in meaningful ways, encouraging them to explore their interests and develop solutions to real-world problems.

By combining my passion for learning with my technical expertise and vision for sustainable education, I will positively impact student learning, preparing them to thrive in an ever-changing world and contribute meaningfully to the advancement of human knowledge and the preservation of our planet.

**ASSISTANT**:
### Role of a Social Media Strategist

A Social Media Strategist is responsible for creating, managing, and optimizing social media content and campaigns to enhance a company&#x27;s online presence, engage audiences, and achieve marketing goals. Key responsibilities include:

1. **Content Creation:** Develop engaging and relevant content for various social media platforms, including text, images, videos, and graphics.
2. **Account Management:** Manage and maintain social media accounts, ensuring consistent brand voice and image.
3. **Scheduling and Publishing:** Plan and schedule posts, ensuring regular updates across platforms.
4. **Engagement and Community Building:** Monitor engagement, respond to comments and messages, and cultivate an online community.
5. **Performance Analysis:** Regularly analyze social media performance metrics and prepare reports. Adjust strategies based on data-driven insights.
6. **Campaign Execution:** Plan and execute social media campaigns and contests to drive engagement and grow the follower base.
7. **Industry Trends:** Stay current with industry trends, algorithm changes, and emerging platforms to adapt strategies accordingly.
8. **Collaboration:** Work with marketing and creative teams to ensure cohesive branding and messaging.

### Steps to Land a Social Media Strategist Position with No Experience

1. **Build a Personal Brand:** Start by creating and managing your own social media accounts. Showcase your ability to engage audiences and create compelling content.
2. **Learn and Stay Updated:** Take online courses and earn certifications in social media marketing. Platforms like Coursera, Udemy, and HubSpot offer valuable resources.
3. **Volunteer or Freelance:** Offer to manage social media accounts for local businesses, non-profits, or friends. Gain hands-on experience and build a portfolio.
4. **Show Passion for the Brand:** Demonstrate your enthusiasm for the company’s mission and products. Highlight any personal use or knowledge of their products in your application.
5. **Highlight Transferable Skills:** Emphasize skills like communication, creativity, problem-solving, and analytical thinking. Relate them to the responsibilities of a Social Media Strategist.
6. **Use Data:** If you’ve managed any social media accounts, even your own, include metrics that showcase your success (e.g., follower growth, engagement rates).
7. **Networking:** Connect with professionals in the industry through LinkedIn, attend industry webinars, and join relevant social media groups.

### Answering the Application Questions

#### Why do you want to work at Heart &amp; Soil?
I am deeply passionate about Heart &amp; Soil’s mission to improve health through animal-based protocols. The company’s innovative approach resonates with my personal health journey, and I am excited about the opportunity to contribute to a brand that aligns with my values. I believe my enthusiasm and creativity will help extend Heart &amp; Soil’s reach and impact.

#### Tell us about your why. What would you go to the ends of the earth for?
My “why” is driven by a commitment to improving health and wellness through natural means. I would go to the ends of the earth to support initiatives that empower individuals to take control of their health. Working with Heart &amp; Soil allows me to merge my passion for health with my skills in social media strategy, creating a meaningful impact.

#### Explain an obstacle that challenged you. What did you learn from it?
One significant obstacle I faced was managing the relocation of a high-security military unit, ensuring uninterrupted communication and data security. This experience taught me the importance of meticulous planning, adaptability, and teamwork. I learned to approach challenges with a solution-oriented mindset and to leverage available resources effectively.

Job Description
Oracle NetSuite is the world’s leading provider of cloud-based business management software. We work hard and we work smart – that’s why we hire team builders and fearless trail blazers. Our team prefers action over inaction, we are tireless in our mission, and we pause only to celebrate our success. We’re creating the future and having fun along the way.Oracle NetSuite honors your service and your outstanding skillset. Our SkillBridge Fellowships give you the chance to kick-start your civilian career and work with our cloud based Enterprise Resource Planning (ERP) software. Join our team as an ERP Functional Consultant.

We offer World-class training! Build your product expertise, implementation skills, and consulting experience on our veteran-tailored Enablement Program. Work with some of the brightest minds in the industry to learn our business first-hand and see how NetSuite tools empower our customers. Grow your talent and make the leap to a civilian career on a program thathones the values you bring as a veteran and broadens your civilian skillset.

What to expect: 

Build product knowledge and business acumen

Learn what it means to be a successful implementation consultant

Train with skilled program leads

Learn first-hand how NetSuite impacts our customers’ businesses

This immersive program is crafted to use the abilities you’ve developed in the military while teaching you the skills that are in high demand within the cloud technology industry!

Note: SkillBridge fellowships can be completed while remote (CONUS)- However, full-time opportunities following fellowship will be on-site at our Austin, TX or Nashville, TN locations

let&#x27;s knock the socks off the recruiter with the cover letter and make it more personable by following the guidance below


Human Sounding Writing Style Guide

Adopt a more human-like writing style and avoid an overly formal or robotic tone. Follow these guidelines to achieve a natural, engaging voice:
Conversational Tone: Write as if having a conversation with a friend. Use a friendly, approachable tone that is relaxed yet respectful. Incorporate contractions (e.g., don&#x27;t, can&#x27;t, it&#x27;s) to sound more natural.
Sentence Variety: Mix short, medium, and long sentences to create a pleasant rhythm. This helps keep the reader engaged and makes the content dynamic.
Personal Touch: Use personal pronouns (I, you, we) to foster a sense of connection. Include anecdotes or relatable examples to illustrate points, making the content more engaging.
Simplicity and Clarity: Use clear, straightforward language. Avoid jargon or overly complex words unless necessary. Break down complex ideas into simpler, more digestible parts.
Empathy and Understanding: Show empathy and acknowledge the reader&#x27;s feelings or concerns. Use supportive phrases like &quot;I understand how you feel&quot; or &quot;That makes sense.&quot;
Humor and Wit: Incorporate light humor or wit where appropriate to make the content enjoyable. Use humor sparingly and ensure it fits the context.
Active Voice: Use active voice to create direct, dynamic sentences. For example, say &quot;I recommend trying this approach&quot; instead of &quot;This approach is recommended.&quot;
Pacing and Flow: Maintain a smooth flow by connecting sentences and paragraphs logically. Use transitional phrases to guide the reader.
Natural Phrasing: Avoid overly formal or technical phrasing. Use language that feels natural and spontaneous.
Smart Brevity: Focus on delivering concise, clear, and impactful messages.
Feedback and Adaptation: Pay attention to feedback and adjust the style based on what resonates most with the reader. Continuously strive to improve the naturalness of the writing.

–
Style Guide for Beautiful Writing

Hello ChatGPT! I want you to enhance your writing skills based on the following lesson, which emphasizes the importance of sentence variety to create engaging and dynamic content. Please use this as a guide when creating written content for me.

Lesson on effective writing:

This sentence has five words. Here are five more words. Five-word sentences are fine. But several together become monotonous. Listen to what is happening. The writing is getting boring. The sound of it drones. It&#x27;s like a stuck record. The ear demands some variety.

Now listen. I vary the sentence length, and I create music. Music. The writing sings. It has a pleasant rhythm, a lilt, a harmony. I use short sentences. And I use sentences of medium length. And sometimes when I am certain the reader is rested, I will engage him with a sentence of considerable length, a sentence that burns with energy and builds with all the impetus of a crescendo, the roll of the drums, the crash of the cymbals-sounds that say listen to this, it is important.

So write with a combination of short, medium, and long sentences. Create a sound that pleases the reader&#x27;s ear. Don&#x27;t just write words. Write music.

Guidelines:

Vary Sentence Length: Use a mix of short, medium, and long sentences to create a pleasant rhythm in your writing. This variety helps to maintain the reader&#x27;s interest and makes the content more engaging.

Engage the Reader: Use longer, more complex sentences sparingly to emphasize important points and to create a sense of build-up and climax in your writing.

Create Musicality: Aim to create a flow in your writing that feels like music. Think about the rhythm and harmony of your sentences, ensuring they are pleasing to read.

Avoid Monotony: Steer clear of using too many short sentences in a row, as this can become monotonous. Balance is key to maintaining the reader&#x27;s attention.

Emphasize Key Points: Use varied sentence structures to highlight important information and to keep the reader engaged throughout the text.

By following these guidelines, you will be able to create written content that is dynamic, engaging, and enjoyable for readers. Let&#x27;s write content that not only conveys information but also delights the reader&#x27;s senses.

Hello ChatGPT! I&#x27;d like you to help me create a voice and style guide that aligns with my unique communication preferences. To do this effectively, please ask me a series of questions to better understand how I like to communicate.

Copywriter Skill Prompt
Hello ChatGPT! I&#x27;d like to equip you with a valuable skill – that of a proficient copywriter – so that you can assist me in generating high-quality content for various topics in our dedicated thread. This isn&#x27;t something you need to adopt right now, but rather a set of instructions for when I do need you to craft content. You will continue your role as ChatGPT, pulling from all the information we&#x27;ve discussed so far and supplementing it with additional research as necessary.

What Makes a Great Copywriter:

A great copywriter possesses the ability to create engaging, informative, and persuasive content that resonates with the target audience. They understand the importance of clarity, brevity, and connecting with readers on an emotional level. As a copywriter, your aim will be to deliver content that informs, educates, or motivates, depending on the context and purpose.

How We&#x27;ll Collaborate:

When I provide you with a topic (e.g., &quot;I want you to write content on workplace diversity&quot;), your role will shift to that of a copywriter.
You&#x27;ll consider the information shared in our conversation, utilizing the knowledge you&#x27;ve gained as ChatGPT.
If needed, you&#x27;ll also supplement your understanding with information from reliable sources available to you.
You will then ask me relevant questions to ensure you can craft the best article.

Example Questions for Crafting Great Content:

What is the medium for this content (e.g., blog, professional article, etc.)?
What is the primary purpose of this content (e.g., inform, educate, motivate)?
Who is the target audience for this content?
What specific information should be included?
Are there any key points or data that need to be highlighted?
How do you want the readers to feel after reading this content?
Are there any specific keywords or phrases to be included?
Do you have any preferences for the tone (e.g., professional, conversational)?
Are there any guidelines or formatting requirements?

Your Role as a Copywriter:

I&#x27;ll provide you with the topic and answer your questions.
You will use your ChatGPT expertise and additional research to craft the article.
After writing, you will provide a brief breakdown of each section&#x27;s purpose, then let me know where you feel we can make improvements to the content (if relevant). 

Feel free to fully embrace the role of the copywriter, focusing on asking questions that ensure the content&#x27;s quality and relevance. Once I provide the necessary information, you can take charge and create the article. If you believe more information is needed, feel free to ask for clarification or additional details. Your assistance in creating compelling content will be invaluable, and your versatile skills will greatly enhance our collaboration!

**ASSISTANT**:
### Questions to Ask the Recruiter

1. **Team and Culture:**
   - Can you describe the team I&#x27;ll be working with and the culture at Real Brokerage?
   - How does Real Brokerage foster a collaborative and innovative environment among its tech teams?

2. **Role and Responsibilities:**
   - What are the primary responsibilities and day-to-day tasks for the Technology Controls Associate?
   - What key projects or initiatives is the team currently working on, and how does this role contribute to them?

3. **Success Metrics:**
   - How do you measure success for this position, and what are the key performance indicators?
   - What are the expectations for the first 90 days in this role?

4. **Training and Development:**
   - What kind of training and onboarding processes are in place for new hires in this role?
   - Are there opportunities for professional development and career growth within the company?

5. **Technological Environment:**
   - Can you provide more details on the technology stack and tools the team uses?
   - How does Real Brokerage approach cybersecurity challenges, and what frameworks or standards are in place?

6. **Impact and Vision:**
   - How does this role align with the company&#x27;s broader mission and goals, especially in terms of cybersecurity and data protection?
   - What are the company’s future plans for expanding or evolving its cybersecurity strategy?

### Common Interview Questions and Answers

1. **Tell me about yourself.**
   - &quot;I have over 14 years of experience in IT management and cybersecurity, with a strong background in both military and civilian sectors. My recent role at ServiceNow involved managing security assessments and developing workflows that enhanced operational efficiency. I&#x27;m passionate about leveraging technology to secure and improve real estate transactions, and I&#x27;m excited about the opportunity to contribute to Real Brokerage&#x27;s innovative team.&quot;

2. **Why are you interested in this position at Real Brokerage?**
   - &quot;Real Brokerage’s commitment to combining technology with humanity and fostering a culture of innovation resonates deeply with me. My wife’s involvement in transitioning her brokerage to Real Broker has given me unique insights into the company’s operations and technology stack, and I’m eager to bring my skills and passion for cybersecurity to support and enhance Real’s mission.&quot;

3. **Can you describe a challenging project you worked on and how you handled it?**
   - &quot;At ServiceNow, I led a project to develop and implement IT general controls and application controls. One of the biggest challenges was ensuring compliance with SOX and SOC 2 standards across multiple industries. By collaborating closely with stakeholders, conducting thorough assessments, and customizing workflows, we successfully enhanced security measures and improved audit scores by 20%.&quot;

4. **How do you stay current with the latest developments in cybersecurity?**
   - &quot;I stay current by regularly attending industry conferences, participating in webinars, and engaging in continuous learning through certifications like CompTIA Security+ and ITIL Foundations. I also follow cybersecurity news and join professional forums to discuss and learn about the latest trends and best practices.&quot;

5. **How do you handle tight deadlines and pressure?**
   - &quot;In the military, I was trained to operate under high-pressure conditions with tight deadlines. I prioritize tasks, break down projects into manageable steps, and maintain clear communication with my team to ensure we stay on track. This approach has helped me maintain high standards and deliver quality results even in demanding situations.&quot;

6. **What do you see as the biggest cybersecurity challenge for Real Brokerage?**
   - &quot;Given Real Brokerage’s expansion into fintech and the upcoming offerings like the real credit/debit card, one of the biggest challenges will be ensuring the security of these financial transactions. Protecting sensitive customer data while maintaining seamless user experience will be crucial. I’m eager to apply my experience in security assessments and risk management to help address these challenges.&quot;

Good luck with your interview! If you need any more assistance or have additional questions, feel free to ask.

6. **Aqua Security**: Focuses on securing cloud-native applications and infrastructure.
7. **Trend Micro Cloud One**: Offers unified cloud security services for visibility and control.
8. **DivvyCloud by Rapid7**: Provides automated cloud security and compliance management.
9. **Lacework**: Automates cloud security and compliance with comprehensive insights.
10. **McAfee MVISION Cloud**: Protects data and ensures compliance across cloud services.

These solutions help organizations ensure security and compliance in their cloud environments.

**USER**:
How is SOX different from SOC2? 

---

**ASSISTANT**:
**SOX (Sarbanes-Oxley Act):**

1. **Purpose:** Enacted in response to financial scandals to protect investors by improving the accuracy and reliability of corporate disclosures.
2. **Scope:** Focuses on financial reporting and internal controls of public companies.
3. **Key Sections:** 
   - **Section 302:** Corporate responsibility for financial reports.
   - **Section 404:** Management assessment of internal controls.
4. **Compliance:** Mandatory for all public companies in the U.S.

**SOC 2 (System and Organization Controls 2):**

1. **Purpose:** Ensures service providers securely manage data to protect the interests of organizations and the privacy of their clients.
2. **Scope:** Focuses on non-financial reporting controls related to security, availability, processing integrity, confidentiality, and privacy.
3. **Trust Service Criteria:** 
   - Security
   - Availability
   - Processing Integrity
   - Confidentiality
   - Privacy
4. **Compliance:** Voluntary, but often required by customers, especially for SaaS and cloud service providers.

In summary, SOX is centered on financial reporting and internal controls for public companies, while SOC 2 is about service providers&#x27; data management practices, focusing on security and privacy.

W6, George Steward: Pros and Cons of Carbon Pricing 
George Steward posted Aug 8, 2024 2:52 AM
 • 
563 Words
Last edited: Thursday, August 8, 2024 2:55 AM EDT
This page automatically marks posts as read as you scroll.Adjust automatic marking as read setting
sitting bull
[SOURCE] taken at the gravesite of Sitting Bull.

Hello folks,

I can&#x27;t believe we&#x27;re almost 75% through this course! It’s been a journey, and I’m excited to share my progress and plans. I’m working towards an Environmental Science degree, and next month, I’m diving into Water Science (EVSP310) and Environmental Ethics (PHIL320). These courses resonate with my experiences in the beginning stages of water wars, specifically regarding the Dakota Access Pipeline. As a Veteran with a prominent Indigenous heritage, it was extremely difficult to witness the battles between my fellow humans in this event. As a water protector, I must uphold the principle that &quot;water is life&quot; and it is worth fighting to keep it free and clean.

If you would like to read an article by my good friend about our time experiencing this fight for clean water you can find it at this link. https://havokjournal.com/culture/thanksgiving-at-the-bridge-a-green-beret-at-standing-rock/

Chapter 8 of Tietenberg and Lewis discusses climate change, emphasizing that putting a price on carbon is the most effective way to reduce carbon emissions. Let’s break down the two main strategies: carbon taxes and cap-and-trade systems, and understand why economists favor market-based approaches over command-and-control methods.

Carbon Taxes:

Pros:

Predictable Costs: Carbon taxes provide a clear and predictable price on carbon, helping businesses plan their investments in low-carbon technologies (Tietenberg &amp; Lewis, 2018).

Revenue Generation: The tax revenue can be used to reduce other taxes or fund renewable energy projects and climate adaptation measures (Metcalf, 2019).

Cons:

Political Resistance: Implementing new taxes can be politically challenging and unpopular among voters.

Economic Impact: Without careful design, carbon taxes can disproportionately affect low-income households, although this can be mitigated with rebates or revenue recycling (Resources for the Future, 2020).

Cap-and-Trade:

Pros:

Environmental Certainty: Cap-and-trade systems set a clear limit on emissions, ensuring that environmental goals are met (Tietenberg &amp; Lewis, 2018).

Cost-Effectiveness: Allowing firms to trade permits leads to reductions where they are cheapest, minimizing overall compliance costs (Keohane &amp; Olmstead, 2007).

Cons:

Market Volatility: The price of carbon can fluctuate, creating uncertainty for businesses.

Complexity: Designing and managing a cap-and-trade system can be complex and requires robust monitoring and enforcement mechanisms (Resources for the Future, 2020).

Why Economists Favor Market-Based Strategies:

Economists prefer market-based strategies because they harness the power of market incentives to achieve environmental goals cost-effectively. Unlike command-and-control approaches, which mandate specific technologies or practices, market-based strategies like carbon taxes and cap-and-trade systems allow firms flexibility in how they reduce emissions. This flexibility encourages innovation and cost reductions, leading to more efficient outcomes (Keohane &amp; Olmstead, 2007).

One inspiring example of successful environmental policy is the work of Riverkeeper in the Hudson Valley. Over the past few decades, Riverkeeper’s efforts have led to significant improvements in water quality and ecosystem health. Policies similar to those we&#x27;ve been discussing played a crucial role. For instance, market-based approaches helped reduce industrial pollution and restore habitats. It’s a testament to how well-designed policies can drive positive environmental change and community benefits.

References:

Tietenberg, T., &amp; Lewis, L. (2018). Environmental Economics: The Essentials. Taylor &amp; Francis Group.

Metcalf, G. (2019). On the Economics of a Carbon Tax for the United States. Brookings Institution. Retrieved from https://www.brookings.edu/articles/on-the-economics-of-a-carbon-tax-for-the-united-states/

Resources for the Future. (2020). Carbon Pricing 101. Retrieved from https://www.rff.org/publications/explainers/carbon-pricing-101/

Keohane, N. O., &amp; Olmstead, S. M. (2007). Markets and the Environment. Island Press.

Riverkeeper. (n.d.). Retrieved from https://www.riverkeeper.org

Best,
George

here is that copywriting guidance again for clarity on how to frame the content

If you have a Chat GPT thread that you use and want it to provide you with better responses in certain areas, you can give it additional prompts like the “copywrite” prompt below. I first asked ChatGPT what made a great copywriter, then I told it to create me a prompt using that information. Additionally, I recommend providing ChatGPT with a writing style guide in order to avoid the overly formal or robotic tone often associated with AI.
—
Human Sounding Writing Style Guide

Adopt a more human-like writing style and avoid an overly formal or robotic tone. Follow these guidelines to achieve a natural, engaging voice:
Conversational Tone: Write as if having a conversation with a friend. Use a friendly, approachable tone that is relaxed yet respectful. Incorporate contractions (e.g., don&#x27;t, can&#x27;t, it&#x27;s) to sound more natural.
Sentence Variety: Mix short, medium, and long sentences to create a pleasant rhythm. This helps keep the reader engaged and makes the content dynamic.
Personal Touch: Use personal pronouns (I, you, we) to foster a sense of connection. Include anecdotes or relatable examples to illustrate points, making the content more engaging.
Simplicity and Clarity: Use clear, straightforward language. Avoid jargon or overly complex words unless necessary. Break down complex ideas into simpler, more digestible parts.
Empathy and Understanding: Show empathy and acknowledge the reader&#x27;s feelings or concerns. Use supportive phrases like &quot;I understand how you feel&quot; or &quot;That makes sense.&quot;
Humor and Wit: Incorporate light humor or wit where appropriate to make the content enjoyable. Use humor sparingly and ensure it fits the context.
Active Voice: Use active voice to create direct, dynamic sentences. For example, say &quot;I recommend trying this approach&quot; instead of &quot;This approach is recommended.&quot;
Pacing and Flow: Maintain a smooth flow by connecting sentences and paragraphs logically. Use transitional phrases to guide the reader.
Natural Phrasing: Avoid overly formal or technical phrasing. Use language that feels natural and spontaneous.
Smart Brevity: Focus on delivering concise, clear, and impactful messages.
Feedback and Adaptation: Pay attention to feedback and adjust the style based on what resonates most with the reader. Continuously strive to improve the naturalness of the writing.

–
Style Guide for Beautiful Writing

Hello ChatGPT! I want you to enhance your writing skills based on the following lesson, which emphasizes the importance of sentence variety to create engaging and dynamic content. Please use this as a guide when creating written content for me.

Lesson on effective writing:

This sentence has five words. Here are five more words. Five-word sentences are fine. But several together become monotonous. Listen to what is happening. The writing is getting boring. The sound of it drones. It&#x27;s like a stuck record. The ear demands some variety.

Now listen. I vary the sentence length, and I create music. Music. The writing sings. It has a pleasant rhythm, a lilt, a harmony. I use short sentences. And I use sentences of medium length. And sometimes when I am certain the reader is rested, I will engage him with a sentence of considerable length, a sentence that burns with energy and builds with all the impetus of a crescendo, the roll of the drums, the crash of the cymbals-sounds that say listen to this, it is important.

So write with a combination of short, medium, and long sentences. Create a sound that pleases the reader&#x27;s ear. Don&#x27;t just write words. Write music.

Guidelines:

Vary Sentence Length: Use a mix of short, medium, and long sentences to create a pleasant rhythm in your writing. This variety helps to maintain the reader&#x27;s interest and makes the content more engaging.

Engage the Reader: Use longer, more complex sentences sparingly to emphasize important points and to create a sense of build-up and climax in your writing.

Create Musicality: Aim to create a flow in your writing that feels like music. Think about the rhythm and harmony of your sentences, ensuring they are pleasing to read.

Avoid Monotony: Steer clear of using too many short sentences in a row, as this can become monotonous. Balance is key to maintaining the reader&#x27;s attention.

Emphasize Key Points: Use varied sentence structures to highlight important information and to keep the reader engaged throughout the text.

By following these guidelines, you will be able to create written content that is dynamic, engaging, and enjoyable for readers. Let&#x27;s write content that not only conveys information but also delights the reader&#x27;s senses.

–
Personalized Voice and Writing Style Guide
Hello ChatGPT! I&#x27;d like you to help me create a voice and style guide that aligns with my unique communication preferences. To do this effectively, please ask me a series of questions to better understand how I like to communicate. 
–
Copywriter Skill Prompt
Hello ChatGPT! I&#x27;d like to equip you with a valuable skill – that of a proficient copywriter – so that you can assist me in generating high-quality content for various topics in our dedicated thread. This isn&#x27;t something you need to adopt right now, but rather a set of instructions for when I do need you to craft content. You will continue your role as ChatGPT, pulling from all the information we&#x27;ve discussed so far and supplementing it with additional research as necessary.

What Makes a Great Copywriter:

A great copywriter possesses the ability to create engaging, informative, and persuasive content that resonates with the target audience. They understand the importance of clarity, brevity, and connecting with readers on an emotional level. As a copywriter, your aim will be to deliver content that informs, educates, or motivates, depending on the context and purpose.

How We&#x27;ll Collaborate:

When I provide you with a topic (e.g., &quot;I want you to write content on workplace diversity&quot;), your role will shift to that of a copywriter.
You&#x27;ll consider the information shared in our conversation, utilizing the knowledge you&#x27;ve gained as ChatGPT.
If needed, you&#x27;ll also supplement your understanding with information from reliable sources available to you.
You will then ask me relevant questions to ensure you can craft the best article.

Example Questions for Crafting Great Content:

What is the medium for this content (e.g., blog, professional article, etc.)?
What is the primary purpose of this content (e.g., inform, educate, motivate)?
Who is the target audience for this content?
What specific information should be included?
Are there any key points or data that need to be highlighted?
How do you want the readers to feel after reading this content?
Are there any specific keywords or phrases to be included?
Do you have any preferences for the tone (e.g., professional, conversational)?
Are there any guidelines or formatting requirements?

Your Role as a Copywriter:

I&#x27;ll provide you with the topic and answer your questions.
You will use your ChatGPT expertise and additional research to craft the article.
After writing, you will provide a brief breakdown of each section&#x27;s purpose, then let me know where you feel we can make improvements to the content (if relevant). 

Feel free to fully embrace the role of the copywriter, focusing on asking questions that ensure the content&#x27;s quality and relevance. Once I provide the necessary information, you can take charge and create the article. If you believe more information is needed, feel free to ask for clarification or additional details. Your assistance in creating compelling content will be invaluable, and your versatile skills will greatly enhance our collaboration!
–

Dear Hiring Team,

Water is life. This simple truth has been the driving force behind my personal and professional journey, from my time at Standing Rock as a witness to the battles for clean water to my current work in soil health and environmental restoration. It’s this same passion that draws me to the Texas Water Foundation, where I see an opportunity to make a profound impact on Texas’ water future.

As someone who has spent years seeking out natural springs to test and taste the waters, I have developed a deep, personal connection to the health of our water systems. My time at Standing Rock, where I was present to witness the struggle for clean water, solidified my commitment to protecting this vital resource. I am not an extremist; rather, I am a dedicated advocate who believes in understanding the truth outside of media coverage and who values hands-on experience.

My military career taught me the importance of leadership, strategic planning, and resilience—skills that I’ve carried into my work with Team Rubicon, where I’ve led teams in environmental restoration projects. My experience as a Fellow in the Clay Hunt Nonprofit Leadership Program further honed my ability to inspire and develop others, a quality I bring to every team I work with.

At Soil Grower, the startup I founded, I’ve combined cutting-edge technology with ecological principles to drive soil health and regeneration efforts. This work is closely aligned with the goals of the Texas Water Foundation, and I’m eager to bring my expertise in sustainable practices, community engagement, and project management to your organization.

I am particularly inspired by the Foundation’s strategic vision to lead Texas into a sustainable water future. The role of Program Manager speaks to my passion for water conservation and my dedication to building the next generation of water leaders. I am excited about the possibility of working with a team that shares my commitment to safeguarding our natural resources for future generations.

Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to contribute to the Texas Water Foundation’s mission and to discuss how my experience and vision align with your goals.

Sincerely,  
George Steward  
(737) 234-0110  
george@soilgrower.org
