Job description:
Grants Manager
 Save Job
TreeFolks

Austin, Texas

 
Job Type	Permanent
Salary Details	$70,000-$73,000
Required Experience	2 - 6 years
TreeFolks is an Austin-based nonprofit organization. Our mission is to empower Central Texans to build stronger communities through planting and caring for trees. TreeFolks is seeking a Grants Manager. This position will contribute to the organization’s mission by managing the grant writing efforts, leading the grant team by overseeing the Grants Assistant, coordinating with program, administrative, and communications staff to ensure grant compliance, and representing the organization with foundations, funders, and other partners.

The person we will add to our active and inclusive team is organized, driven, hardworking, and can work within TreeFolks’ Core Values. The ideal candidate has extensive experience with prospecting, writing and managing local, state, federal, and foundation grants and is extremely self-motivated and ambitious with a proven record of success. Please see below for a full description of duties and qualifications. 

Duties will include, but are not limited to:

Lead the process of grant submission, including prospecting, determining the relevance of opportunities, working with other staff to develop proposals and budgets, write narrative, establish metrics, and submit proposals in a timely manner, and tracking submissions and responses. 
Maintain proficient knowledge of the organization&#x27;s history, programs and annual goals to represent accurately in proposals and verbal communications. 
Maintain an up-to-date database and records of all current and historical grant proposals, including contact information, submission dates, budget amount, purpose of funding, related correspondence, proposal status, reporting timelines, and other important dates.
Build and manage relationships with representatives of current and potential grant-making organizations.
Provide information via meetings or other forms of communication to staff, Board, partners, and other stakeholders regarding grants, such as facilitating grant kick-off meetings; and representing the organization in meetings regarding grants facilitated by other organizations.
Submit all required reports and compliance documentation and ensure the accuracy of invoices for grants. 
Serve as the organizational expert on grants and provide guidance to other staff, including the Grants Assistant, as needed.
Assist Deputy Director with drafting municipal contract proposals, as needed. 
The ideal candidate will have the following qualifications:

Significant professional experience and proven success in grant prospecting, writing, and management. 
Self-motivated with the ability to prioritize and manage multiple tasks with minimal supervision
Experience managing local, state, and federal grants. 
Outstanding record-keeping, time management, and written and oral communications skills.
Administrative and organizational management experience, including budget oversight, operational and strategic planning, and human resources.
Experience with digital tools such as Google Drive, AirTable, and CRM applications.
Bachelor’s degree preffered, but can be substituted for extensive professional experience.
An ability to support and motivate team members.
A background working in a dynamic, high-energy team environment.
Demonstrated interest in the mission, vision and values of TreeFolks
TreeFolks considers the job qualifications as a guide and not an absolute list. We encourage all candidates who feel they meet the spirit of the job description, are passionate about our mission and core values, and can do the work to apply. 

This is a full time, permanent position with a mix of in-office work, remote work, and working on-site at events. TreeFolks offers a competitive salary, plus health benefits, generous vacation time, flexible schedule, a casual work environment, and professional development opportunities. The starting salary ranges from  based on experience, qualifications, and additional attributes, such as bilingual or firsthand $70,000 to $73,000 knowledge of communities in which TreeFolks works. 

Equity Statement: 

TreeFolks is an equal-opportunity employer committed to building a diverse and inclusive workplace. We welcome and encourage candidates of all backgrounds, including but not limited to, people of color, LGBTQ+ individuals, women, veterans, neurodivergent people, and those with disabilities. TreeFolks will not discriminate against any candidate on the basis of race, sex, gender identity, sexual orientation, class, religion, national origin, disability, age, and/or genetic information. 

HOW TO APPLY
To apply, please visit our application portal and upload a letter of interest, resume, and three references with contact information.

Application deadline: open until filled 

Anticipated start date: September 5, 2024 

When you apply, please indicate that you are responding to the posting on Conservation Job Board.

Dear Water Leaders Hiring Team,

Water is life. This simple truth has been a driving force behind my personal and professional journey, from my time at Standing Rock as a witness to the battles for clean water to my current work in soil health and environmental restoration. It’s this same passion that draws me to the Texas Water Foundation, where I see an opportunity to make a profound impact on Texas’ water future.

As someone who has spent years seeking out natural springs to test and taste the waters, I have developed a deep, personal connection to the health of our water systems. My time at Standing Rock, where I was present to witness the struggle for clean water, solidified my commitment to protecting this vital resource. I am not an extremist; rather, I am a dedicated advocate who believes in understanding the truth outside of media coverage and who values hands-on experience.

My military career taught me the importance of leadership, strategic planning, and resilience—skills that I’ve carried into my volunteer work with Team Rubicon, where I’ve led teams in disaster relief and environmental restoration projects. My experience as a Fellow in the Clay Hunt Nonprofit Leadership Program further honed my ability to inspire and develop others, a quality I bring to every team I work with.

At Soil Grower, the startup I founded, I’ve combined cutting-edge technology with ecological principles to drive soil health and regeneration efforts. This work is closely aligned with the goals of the Texas Water Foundation, and I’m eager to bring my expertise in sustainable practices, community engagement, and project management to your organization.

I have written several grant proposals and have a strong foundation in researching and identifying grant opportunities across various industries. While I’m still building my experience in grant writing, I have a natural aptitude for understanding the process and am eager to fully immerse myself in learning the intricacies of successful fundraising. My proactive approach and passion for supporting environmental initiatives make me confident in my ability to quickly become a valuable asset in securing grants for TreeFolks.

I am particularly inspired by the Foundation’s strategic vision to lead Texas into a sustainable water future. The role of Program Manager speaks to my passion for water conservation and my dedication to building the next generation of water leaders. I am excited about the possibility of working with a team that shares my commitment to safeguarding our natural resources for future generations.

Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to contribute to the Texas Water Foundation’s mission and to discuss how my experience and vision align with your goals.

Sincerely,  
George Steward

Position: Program Manager

The Opportunity:

Ohalo is seeking a leader in our organization, to bridge the gap between science and product development, ensuring technical programs align seamlessly with commercial objectives. As program manager you will partner closely with both product leads and science teams to oversee the coordination and execution of programs, manage timelines, and ensure cross-functional alignment. Your role will involve a range of responsibilities, from road mapping and stakeholder management to risk management and conflict resolution. Additionally, you will be responsible for initiating and scoping new programs, developing and managing dashboards, databases, and key metrics to ensure that science-driven product work is on track and delivered on time.

Responsibilities:

Champion and oversee multiple programs from inception to launch, ensuring alignment with strategic objectives and regulatory requirements. Proactively identify and resolve roadblocks, leveraging program management expertise to deliver results.
Play a pivotal role in initiating and scoping new programs, collaborating with stakeholders to define clear objectives, scope, and timelines.
Manage the operational aspects of programs, including meeting facilitation and documentation. Introduce and optimize tools, templates, and processes to empower teams and enhance efficiency.
Play a pivotal role in initiating and scoping new programs, collaborating with stakeholders to define clear objectives, scope, and timelines.
Diligently track program budgets, resources, and key performance metrics. Provide insightful reports to stakeholders, offering proactive guidance and recommendations. Ensure prompt and effective issue resolution and risk mitigation.
Build strong relationships with product leads, collaborating closely to translate scientific discoveries into market-ready products. Ensure technical program goals are aligned with commercial objectives. 
Leverage project management best practices to support the achievement of program goals and objectives.
Candidate Profile 

Bachelor’s degree in a scientific or business discipline. 
Minimum 5 years of professional experience in project management in a research setting, preferably with a consumer products or agricultural company.
Proven experience using project management and dashboard tools including, Miro, Airtable, Looker Studio, Google Suite (Sheets, Slides, etc) preferred.
Project Management (PMP) certification or similar preferred 
Desired Skills/Experience

Intrinsically motivated, taking ownership of responsibilities and demonstrating a strong commitment to personal and professional growth.
Comfortable in making decisions and assumptions in absence of complete data.  Intellectually curious and service oriented.

Effectively influences and guides teams without relying on formal authority.
Proven ability to build strong partnerships with cross-functional stakeholders, particularly product leads.
Capable of leading complex decision-making processes and adeptly navigating and resolving intricate challenges.
Ability to direct, manage, plan and control multiple activities in order to meet deadlines.

About Ohalo: 

Ohalo™ aims to accelerate evolution to unlock nature&#x27;s potential. Founded in 2019, Ohalo develops novel breeding systems and improved plant varieties that help farmers grow more food with fewer natural resources, increasing the yield, resiliency, and genetic diversity of crops to sustainably feed our population. Ohalo&#x27;s breakthrough technology, Boosted Breeding™, will usher in a new era of improved productivity to radically transform global agriculture. For more information, visit www.ohalo.com.

### Role Synopsis and 3-Month, 6-Month, 1-Year, 5-Year Plan

**Role Overview:**
As a Program Manager at Ohalo, your primary responsibility is to bridge the gap between science and product development, ensuring that scientific advancements are translated into market-ready products. You’ll oversee multiple programs, manage timelines, and ensure cross-functional alignment with commercial goals. Your role is pivotal in initiating new programs, managing budgets, tracking key metrics, and facilitating effective communication between stakeholders.

**3-Month Plan:**
- **Orientation and Relationship Building:** Spend the first few weeks understanding the company’s culture, technologies, and strategic goals. Establish strong relationships with key stakeholders, including product leads, scientists, and executives.
- **Program Scoping:** Begin scoping initial programs, setting clear objectives, timelines, and resources required. Get familiar with existing projects and identify any immediate roadblocks or risks.
- **Tool Optimization:** Introduce and optimize project management tools, ensuring they meet the needs of cross-functional teams.

**6-Month Plan:**
- **Program Execution:** Fully manage and oversee the execution of multiple programs, ensuring they are on track to meet their strategic objectives. Begin to see the fruits of the scoping and planning done in the initial months.
- **Team Alignment:** Ensure that all teams are aligned with the commercial objectives, helping to translate scientific discoveries into viable products.
- **Stakeholder Reporting:** Start providing regular updates and reports to stakeholders, offering insights into progress, risks, and mitigation strategies.

**1-Year Plan:**
- **Program Launches:** Successfully launch initial programs, having overseen them from inception to completion. Ensure that these programs align with both scientific goals and commercial needs.
- **Strategic Influence:** Begin to influence long-term strategic planning, using insights gained from the first year to drive the direction of new programs.
- **Process Refinement:** Continuously refine and improve program management processes, tools, and communication strategies to enhance efficiency and effectiveness.

**5-Year Plan:**
- **Long-Term Impact:** Establish yourself as a key leader within Ohalo, driving the evolution of the company’s program management practices. Your efforts will contribute significantly to the development of Ohalo’s product portfolio, impacting global agriculture.
- **Scaling Operations:** Play a crucial role in scaling the company’s operations, ensuring that the program management function can support larger, more complex projects.
- **Innovative Leadership:** Be at the forefront of initiating and driving innovative programs that push the boundaries of Ohalo’s capabilities, keeping the company at the cutting edge of agricultural technology.

### Analysis of Your Work History:

Your background aligns well with the Program Manager role at Ohalo. Here’s how:

1. **Leadership and Project Management:** Your extensive experience in IT management, strategic planning, and leading complex projects aligns with the program management responsibilities at Ohalo. Managing timelines, budgets, and cross-functional teams are core aspects of both your past roles and this position.

2. **Green Industry Expertise:** Your work with Soil Grower and various arborist roles demonstrates your commitment to environmental sustainability. This experience is directly relevant to Ohalo’s mission to enhance agricultural productivity through innovative breeding systems.

3. **Scientific Knowledge and Technical Skills:** While your primary experience is in IT and environmental science, your current studies and focus on soil health, coupled with your technical skills in data-driven decision-making, position you as a candidate capable of bridging the gap between science and product development.

4. **Military Experience:** Your military background has provided you with a strong foundation in leadership, strategic thinking, and operational efficiency—skills that are essential for overseeing multiple programs and driving them to successful completion.

### Crafting Your Application:

To gain Ohalo’s attention, emphasize your unique blend of experience in environmental science, IT, and leadership. Highlight your passion for sustainable agriculture, your ability to manage complex projects, and your commitment to driving ecological success through innovative solutions.

Consider including specific examples of how you’ve successfully managed projects from inception to completion, aligning them with strategic goals—this will resonate with the responsibilities of the Program Manager role. Your interest in polyploidy with algae and your work with Soil Grower can be powerful points to demonstrate your alignment with Ohalo’s mission to accelerate evolution and improve agricultural productivity.

Dear Hiring Team,

I’ve always believed in the potential of nature to solve humanity’s greatest challenges. This belief has driven my journey from a military career to IT management, and now to my true passion—advancing sustainable agricultural practices. When I discovered Ohalo’s mission to unlock nature’s potential through Boosted Breeding™, I felt an immediate connection. The opportunity to contribute as your Program Manager feels like a natural progression in my journey, where I can bring my unique blend of leadership, environmental science expertise, and project management skills to a cause that truly resonates with me.

My work with Soil Grower is a testament to my commitment to sustainability. As the founder, I’ve pioneered the use of cutting-edge technologies to improve soil health and regenerate ecosystems, aligning closely with Ohalo’s goal to enhance agricultural productivity. This role has honed my ability to manage complex projects, collaborate across disciplines, and deliver results that make a tangible impact on our environment.

While my background is deeply rooted in environmental conservation, my experience as a Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army has equipped me with the strategic thinking and leadership skills necessary for the program management role at Ohalo. Leading high-stakes projects under pressure taught me the importance of aligning technical goals with broader mission objectives—a skill I’m eager to bring to your team.

I’m particularly excited about the prospect of driving programs that bridge science and product development at Ohalo. My ability to initiate and scope new programs, coupled with a strong track record in managing budgets, timelines, and cross-functional teams, will ensure that Ohalo’s groundbreaking technologies reach their full potential. Additionally, my passion for polyploidy with algae and other sustainable practices aligns perfectly with your vision to transform global agriculture.

I recognize that program management is as much about the people as it is about the processes. Building strong relationships with product leads, scientists, and stakeholders is a strength of mine, and I’m confident that my approach will foster collaboration and innovation within Ohalo.

In the next three months, I envision diving deep into Ohalo’s existing programs, identifying areas of alignment and opportunities for optimization. By six months, I aim to have key programs on track, with clear roadmaps and stakeholder buy-in. Within a year, I hope to have launched several successful programs, contributing significantly to Ohalo’s strategic goals. Over five years, my goal is to help scale Ohalo’s operations, driving innovation and ensuring that our work has a lasting impact on global agriculture.

Thank you for considering my application. I am eager to contribute to Ohalo’s mission and to discuss how my experience, skills, and passion align with your needs. Together, I believe we can unlock nature’s potential and create a more sustainable future.

Warm regards,

**ASSISTANT**:
Based on the latest information about Ohalo, the company is currently focused on implementing its groundbreaking &quot;Boosted Breeding&quot; technology, which is poised to revolutionize agriculture by dramatically improving crop yields, adaptability, and resilience. This technology allows parent plants to pass their entire genome to offspring, rather than a random selection, leading to significant improvements in genetic diversity, plant health, and productivity. Ohalo has already begun implementing this technology across various crops, including potatoes, corn, and berries, and plans to expand its work to other crops and geographies over the next few years【181†source】【182†source】.

Who We Are
We&#x27;re building the world&#x27;s most trusted public town square—and we pride ourselves on our commitment to protecting free speech within the boundaries of the law. As part of the Safety Org, the Strategic Response Team (SRT) delivers the highest tier of customer support and Terms of Service enforcement at X. SRT manages the most challenging escalations and crises faced by the company with a globally distributed team maintaining 24/7/365, follow-the-sun coverage.

Role: Strategic Response Team: Program Manager I
Location: Austin, TX OR San Jose, CA OR New York, NY

Base Salary Range: $90,000 - $115,000 USD
_

What You Will Do

As an SRT Program Manager, you will support policy and protocol launches, knowledge management, training, quality assurance, and process improvements through data analysis. You will work closely with SRT leadership and cross-functional partners for strategic and operational efforts to develop, implement, and upkeep the support provided to priority X clients/users. 

You will support multi-disciplinary projects and lead moderate complexity projects for SRT, identifying future opportunities and improving processes.

You will plan requirements with internal customers and usher projects through the entire project lifecycle. This includes managing project schedules and clearly communicating them to project stakeholders. 

You will use cross-functional knowledge to understand issues, trends, and perspectives that may influence internal partners and practices.

You will work cross-functionally for strategic and operational efforts that impact the organization, contributing to SRT’s vision. 

You will ensure effective communication, alignment, and execution of the organization’s strategy and roadmap.

Qualifications

3-4 years of work experience in Project Management, preferably in tech/ strategy/product operations, building relationships and supporting operational initiatives. 

Experience managing projects with moderate enterprise initiatives, maintaining effective relationships and collaborating with various cross-functional partners.

Ability to dig deeper to understand underlying issues and translate data into actionable insights to drive improvement across the business.

Experience working with large datasets and SQL to build dashboards and reports, and complete analyses to drive operational improvements.

Ability to put out fires and support the development of risk mitigation strategies.

Ability to work well under pressure and be comfortable working in a fast-paced, ever-changing environment.

Strong research, analytical, investigative and communications skills.

Resourceful and considers cost-benefit tradeoff in all decisions.

**ASSISTANT**:
Over the past five years, I&#x27;ve immersed myself in the study of a remarkable plant species that serves as a living model of resilience, adaptability, and balance. This plant, with over 300 species found on nearly every continent, is a true pioneer in ecosystem establishment. It works symbiotically with trees and mycorrhizal fungi, enhancing photosynthesis, nutrient uptake, water retention, and carbon sequestration. The plant&#x27;s ability to create stasis in biological systems amidst inevitable chaos has led me to explore its potential in addressing one of the most pressing issues of our time: the global fertility crisis.

I&#x27;ve been delving into how this plant substance, an adaptogen, can help restore balance in the human endocrine system by allowing proteins to properly fold, ultimately fostering homeostasis in biological systems. This research has been deeply personal, too. The most poignant example of this balance is seen in my own family, where my last two children were born 1.5 years apart—one on the winter solstice and the other on the summer solstice. The statistical odds of this happening are astronomically low, underscoring the profound impact that balance within biological systems can have on our lives.

This concept of balance extends beyond the natural world. Just as this plant brings harmony to its ecosystem, we can apply these principles to restore peace and balance in the real world and, importantly, in the digital realm. At 𝕏, you&#x27;re building a trusted global digital town square—an environment that faces constant challenges to maintain equilibrium in a space where diverse voices must coexist. **ASSISTANT**:
Reaching out directly to Claire, the Customer Success Manager at SkyFi, is a great approach, especially since you&#x27;ve already established some rapport with the team through your previous interviews. Here’s how you could proceed:

### 1. **Acknowledge Your Previous Interaction**
   - Start by briefly mentioning your previous interview experience with the company. This shows continuity in your interest and commitment to SkyFi.
   
### 2. **Express Enthusiasm for the New Role**
   - Clearly state your interest in the Customer Success Associate position, emphasizing how your skills align with the responsibilities of the role.
   - Mention any relevant skills or experiences you’ve gained since your last interview that make you an even stronger candidate.

### 3. **Connect Your Previous Experience**
   - Relate your previous interview experience to the new role. Mention any insights you gained from those interactions that reaffirm your interest in SkyFi and how they’ve prepared you to excel in the Customer Success role.
   
### 4. **Propose a Conversation**
   - Suggest a brief conversation or meeting to discuss how your background aligns with the needs of the Customer Success team. This shows initiative and eagerness to contribute to the team’s success.

### 5. **Thank Her for the Opportunity**
   - Close by thanking Claire for her time and consideration, reinforcing your enthusiasm for the role.

Here’s a sample message to get you started:

---

**Subject: Re: Expressing Interest in the Customer Success Associate Position**

Hi Claire,

I hope you’re doing well! Earlier this year, I had the pleasure of interviewing with several members of the SkyFi team for a Sales Admin role. I enjoyed learning more about the company and the culture, and the experience only deepened my admiration for the innovative work SkyFi is doing.

I recently came across the opening for a Customer Success Associate and was immediately excited. Given my background in [mention any relevant experience or skills], I believe I could make a meaningful impact on the Customer Success team. My previous interviews with the SkyFi team have given me valuable insights into the company’s goals and challenges, which I’m eager to support in this new capacity.

If you’re available, I’d love to discuss how I could contribute to the success of the Customer Success team. I’m confident that my passion for customer satisfaction, combined with my understanding of SkyFi’s mission, would make me a strong fit for this role.

Thank you for considering my application, and I look forward to the possibility of reconnecting!

Best regards,  
George Steward

Customer Success Associate
Location
Our headquarters is in Austin, Texas, but remote employment is possible anywhere in the world. We are a global team and want you to work wherever you feel most productive.

Our Mission
We&#x27;re unlocking the secrets of our planet. SkyFi simplifies obtaining high-resolution Earth observation data and analytics, ensuring businesses and professionals a seamless and efficient user experience. No more complex procedures or hefty price tags. We&#x27;re empowering everyone, from individuals to companies, to understand and utilize the power of space for good.

What we do has tremendous potential to solve meaningful problems in our world. This technology is a powerful tool for enterprises and individuals, enabling them to leverage satellite imagery and analytics for critical applications such as assessing the structural integrity of bridges to prevent failures, monitoring crop health for optimized agricultural output, tracking endangered species for environmental conservation, and exploring a myriad of other innovative use cases yet to be discovered. Grab the chance to be part of this. Join a team of open-minded, dynamic people solving new challenges and working on new technology in an exciting market with immense growth. SkyFi is the place for you. 

The Job
As a Customer Success Associate, you will play a key role in ensuring that our enterprise customers successfully integrate and utilize SkyFi’s geospatial data and analytics solutions to meet their specific goals. You will be responsible for collaborating with our sales team to onboard new customers and nurture their long-term relationship with SkyFi, including enabling successful platform use, addressing inquiries, and collaborating with internal teams to ensure an exceptional customer experience. This position is ideal for someone passionate about technology and customer service and who has 1-2 years of experience in a customer-facing role.

Serve as the primary point of contact for a portfolio of customers, guiding them through the SkyFi platform and ensuring their long-term success with our geospatial data and analytics products​​.

Collaborate with our sales team to uphold and improve processes to ensure both parties thoroughly understand customer needs and opportunities. 

Provide robust and customized onboarding to new customers, helping them understand how to maximize their use of our tools, features, and product capabilities​.

Thoroughly understand SkyFi business operations, including image processing, billing, customer support, and the SkyFi platform to provide timely and creative solutions. 

Continuously search for opportunities for growth within a customer relationship and maintain strong communication with the dedicated sales team member to capitalize on these opportunities.

Address customer inquiries and troubleshoot issues, collaborating with technical teams to ensure timely resolution​.

Proactively monitor customer accounts and orders to anticipate needs, provide solutions, and ensure satisfaction​​.

Collaborate with internal teams (sales, product, and engineering) to improve the customer experience based on feedback and data-driven insights​.

Manage customer communications via email, chat, and phone to ensure responsiveness and alignment with customer expectations.

Assist in creating educational resources, including tutorials, webinars, and knowledge-base articles​.

What We Are Looking For
A natural passion to exceed customer expectations and build strong relationships.

Minimum of 1-2 years of experience in customer success, support, or a related customer-facing role.

Excellent communication and interpersonal skills with the ability to explain technical concepts to non-technical users​.

Strong problem-solving skills and the ability to work independently.

Experience with SaaS platforms or technology products is a plus, including but not limited to Google Workspace, Hubspot, Stripe, and Zendesk.

Ability to multitask and prioritize in a fast-paced environment​.

Familiarity with geospatial data, analytics, or Earth Observation technology is a plus but not required​​.

At SkyFi You Will
Be well compensated. Possibility for equity. The expected salary for the role is $60,000.

Receive best-in-class benefits, including premium medical, dental, and vision coverage, 20 days paid time off, and parental leave.

Play a critical role in building a market-changing product in the exciting realm of space.

Thrive in a fast-paced, dynamic environment that rewards initiative, innovation, and getting things done.

Have the flexibility to work anywhere in the world.

SkyFi is an equal opportunity employer that values and encourages workplace diversity.

### 1. How My Experience Aligns with the Network Administrator Role

My diverse background in IT management, network security, and technology integration positions me as a strong candidate for the Network Administrator role at Liberty Hill ISD. Here’s how my experience aligns with the responsibilities of the position:

**Technical Leadership and Network Management:**  
I have a proven track record of leading IT teams and managing complex network infrastructures, ensuring seamless operations and robust security. For example, during my time as Chief Information Systems Technician in the U.S. Army, I was responsible for maintaining a secure and stable network environment that supported over 800 personnel in high-pressure situations. This experience directly aligns with the primary purpose of this role—maintaining a stable, efficient, and secure network infrastructure for the district.

**Project Coordination and Implementation:**  
My experience in overseeing large-scale IT projects, such as migrating data services and upgrading network systems, has honed my ability to manage multiple projects simultaneously while ensuring alignment with strategic goals. My role in managing the relocation of the 7th Special Forces Group&#x27;s IT infrastructure from Fort Bragg to Eglin AFB required close coordination with multiple stakeholders, including vendors, contractors, and internal teams. This aligns with the need to work as a project coordinator interfacing with consultants, architects, and contractors for ongoing and planned construction, additions, and/or renovations within the district.

**Security and Compliance Expertise:**  
Throughout my career, I have consistently prioritized cybersecurity, implementing intrusion detection systems, conducting forensic analysis, and ensuring compliance with various security protocols. My knowledge of CISA guidelines and best practices, combined with my hands-on experience in network security, would allow me to develop and implement best practices related to network and information security, as outlined in the job description.

**Customer Service and Communication:**  
My ability to communicate technical information effectively to both technical and non-technical personnel has been a cornerstone of my career. Whether it&#x27;s providing high-quality customer service, supporting end-users, or liaising with vendors, I’ve consistently delivered solutions that meet the needs of the organization. This experience would enable me to excel in providing technical support and working cooperatively with end-users to resolve problems efficiently.

### 2. Impact on Student Learning in this Role

As a Network Administrator, my impact on student learning would be realized through the following key areas:

**Ensuring Reliable Access to Educational Resources:**  
By maintaining and optimizing the district&#x27;s network infrastructure, I would ensure that students and teachers have uninterrupted access to digital learning resources. A stable network is crucial for the effective use of educational technology in the classroom, enabling students to engage with interactive lessons, access online research materials, and collaborate on projects.

**Enhancing Security and Privacy:**  
In today’s digital age, protecting student data is paramount. My background in cybersecurity ensures that the network will be safeguarded against potential breaches, protecting sensitive information and providing a safe digital environment for students to learn and explore. This protection is not just about compliance; it&#x27;s about fostering trust and confidence in the district&#x27;s technology systems.

**Supporting Innovative Teaching Methods:**  
With a robust and flexible network in place, teachers can incorporate a variety of digital tools and platforms into their teaching, enhancing student engagement and fostering a more dynamic learning environment. My role would be to ensure that the network can support these innovative approaches, enabling educators to use technology to its fullest potential.

**Promoting Equity in Education:**  
By ensuring that all students have reliable access to the district’s digital resources, regardless of their location or socioeconomic status, I would contribute to closing the digital divide. Every student deserves the opportunity to benefit from modern educational tools, and a well-maintained network is the foundation for making that a reality.

In summary, my experience and dedication to technology, security, and education uniquely position me to positively impact student learning in the Liberty Hill ISD. By leveraging my skills and expertise, I would contribute to creating an environment where technology enhances educational outcomes and prepares students for future success.

Senior Business Consultant -  Land and Property Design

As a Senior Business Consultant - Land and Property Design at 5th World, you will play a pivotal role in guiding our clients toward implementing regenerative systems, ecosystem restoration, renewable energies, and advanced water management practices. Your expertise will be instrumental in assisting farmers, landowners, and organizations in transitioning from conventional practices to a wide array of best-in-class principles, including regenerative agriculture, permaculture, conservation, earthworks, agrivoltaics, CEA, agroforestry, and agroecology.

You will be responsible for providing strategic advice, conducting comprehensive assessments, designing innovative concepts, master and implementation plans, and fostering long-term relationships with clients. This position requires a blend of consulting experience, project management skills, and the ability to develop and maintain client relationships. The ideal candidate will demonstrate strong analytical abilities, effective communication, and a proactive approach to problem-solving and project execution.


Key Responsibilities
Client Engagement and Relationship Management:

Serve as a primary point of contact for clients, ensuring clear and effective communication.
Understand client needs and objectives to provide tailored consulting solutions.
Build and maintain strong relationships with clients, fostering trust and satisfaction.
Project Management and Execution:

Assist in the planning, execution, and delivery of consulting projects.
Manage project timelines, budgets, and resources to ensure successful completion.
Conduct project reviews and provide regular updates to clients and senior management.
Analysis and Problem Solving:

Conduct detailed analyses to identify client challenges and opportunities.
Develop actionable recommendations and solutions based on data and client insights.
Utilize industry best practices and methodologies to deliver high-quality outcomes.
Sales Support and Proposal Development:

Contribute to the development of proposals, presentations, and sales materials.
Assist in identifying new business opportunities and support sales efforts.
Collaborate with senior consultants to develop strategic proposals tailored to client needs.
Quality Assurance:

Ensure all project deliverables meet quality standards and client expectations.
Conduct quality checks and reviews on work produced by junior consultants and team members.
Provide constructive feedback to enhance the overall quality of consulting services.
Continuous Learning and Development:

Stay updated with industry trends, methodologies, and best practices.
Participate in training and development programs to enhance consulting skills and knowledge.
Share insights and knowledge with the team to foster a collaborative learning environment.
Operational Efficiency:

Assist in developing and implementing standard operating procedures (SOPs) for consulting processes.
Identify opportunities to streamline workflows and enhance operational efficiency.
Utilize technology and tools to improve productivity and project management.



What Success Looks Like
Client Satisfaction: Achieving high levels of client satisfaction through effective communication, timely project delivery, and quality outcomes.
Project Success: Successfully completing projects on time, within scope, and budget, with positive client feedback.
Professional Growth: Continuously improving consulting skills, knowledge, and career development.
Operational Excellence: Implementing efficient and streamlined processes that contribute to the overall success of consulting services.
Other Responsibilities

Assist in developing and delivering training sessions and workshops for clients.
Provide clients with tools and knowledge to maximize the benefits of consulting services.

Conduct research to understand industry trends and client challenges.

Ensure compliance with company policies and industry regulations.

Share insights and best practices to enhance the overall quality of consulting services.

About 5th World
5th World Mission and Vision

5th World is on a mission to accelerate the world&#x27;s transition to regenerative and distributed energy, water and food systems.

We envision a world built upon autonomous regenerative communities and properties fostering harmony among technology, nature and humanity.

5th World Philosophy and Core Values

5th World’s philosophy is based on the principles of capitalism, freedom and liberty, individual sovereignty and enlightened self-interest. At 5th World, we aim to find profitable solutions that lead to win-win situations and generate positive externalities for our societies and for the planet, while respecting the free choice of individuals and communities.

5th World is an apolitical** organization built upon core values &amp; principles.

Core Values:

Integrity &amp; Respect: Behaving ethically and doing the right thing. Leading by example.
Empathy: Ability to take on another&#x27;s perspective, to understand, feel, and share compassion and respond to their experience.
Trusting: Operating with good intentions to create space for vulnerability. Leading with trust.
Optimism: Embracing a positive outlook and focusing on the possibilities. Believing in a brighter future and maintaining a hopeful and confident attitude in the face of challenges.
Core Principles:

Active Listening: Suspending our judgement in a way that encourages others to share their opinions and allows us to hear what others are truly saying.
Straight Talk: Respectfully saying the things that we really mean in a timely manner. Providing feedback and being committed to having the conversations that are needed.
Growth Mindset: Seeing opportunities for improvement and progress in every situation, embracing our failures and encouraging continuous learning  and adaptation.
** Politics, religion and social issues have become topics that are divisive and affect the rights of others. 5th World’s policy is to not support or participate in political, religious or social matters.

Dear 5th World Hiring Team,

I am writing to express my profound interest in joining 5th World as a Senior Business Consultant in Land and Property Design. From the moment I learned about 5th World’s mission—to accelerate the transition to regenerative systems—I knew I had found an organization that aligns perfectly with my life’s work and passion. As the founder of Soil Grower, I have spent the last several years immersed in designing and implementing regenerative systems that harness the power of nature and technology to heal ecosystems, restore biodiversity, and ensure a sustainable future.

For me, regeneration is more than just a career—it&#x27;s a calling. My Native American heritage has instilled in me a deep respect for nature and a commitment to preserving the balance of ecosystems. I believe that the principles of biomimicry, which have guided my work at Soil Grower, are essential to creating closed-loop systems that benefit both people and the planet. I have been particularly focused on the integration of Earth Power Lodge systems, which I believe could significantly enhance 5th World&#x27;s efforts to build resilient communities. By combining these systems with community cooperatives, we can empower landowners and farmers to generate renewable energy and create regenerative living systems that sustain their livelihoods.

In my consulting work, I have advised clients on implementing regenerative systems across various environments. From designing animal shelters that optimize natural cycles to building solar-powered farms, my work has always focused on creating systems that mirror nature’s processes. I bring a wealth of experience in soil health, water management, and agroforestry that I believe will be instrumental in driving 5th World’s mission forward.

The prospect of using my personal projects—such as my current plans for a 6.1-acre property in La Grange, NY—as a showcase for 5th World’s regenerative systems excites me. This property presents an ideal opportunity to demonstrate the synergy between nature and technology and create content that amplifies 5th World’s brand and mission.

I am eager to contribute to 5th World’s vision of a world where technology and nature work together in harmony. My entrepreneurial spirit, deep knowledge of regenerative practices, and passion for building resilient systems align perfectly with your mission. Together, I am confident we can accelerate the transition to a regenerative future, ensuring that communities not only survive but thrive.

Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to contribute to the incredible work 5th World is doing.

**George Steward**

Dear 5th World Hiring Team,

I’m writing with a heart full of excitement and ambition to express my interest in joining 5th World as a Senior Business Consultant in Land and Property Design. From the moment I learned about your mission to accelerate regenerative and distributed energy, water, and food systems, I felt a deep resonance with your work. This role aligns not only with my professional experience but with my life’s purpose—bridging the gap between technology and nature to build thriving, sustainable communities.

As the founder of **Soil Grower**, I’ve focused on the principles of biomimicry, creating solutions that accelerate natural processes. My work is deeply personal, inspired by a drive to reconnect humanity with the earth in a meaningful way. I’ve designed animal shelters, integrated sustainable practices into my projects, and developed closed-loop systems using biostimulants to foster biodiversity. My passion for trees and soil health has also led me to pursue my arborist certification while expanding my knowledge of agroforestry and regenerative agriculture.

What excites me most about joining 5th World is the chance to take this passion further—contributing to projects that don’t just sustain but regenerate ecosystems. I envision collaborating with you to integrate **Earth Power Lodges** (EPLs) into community cooperative models. These lodges could generate income while empowering local communities with the resources to extend their regenerative practices. I believe these systems can be transformational, turning entire neighborhoods into networks of regenerative living, with soil regeneration and decentralized energy at the heart of their success.

While I’m still working toward finishing my environmental science degree, my academic journey has always been driven by an insatiable thirst for knowledge—building upon the practical experience I’ve already gained. Whether it’s solar farms, water management, or soil health, I’ve always approached each subject with humility and hunger. I may not have all the answers now, but I know how to seek them out and I’m always eager to learn.

Personally, my deep connection to nature stems from my **Native American heritage**, which has shaped my understanding of the interconnectedness of all life. This connection is more than a philosophy—it’s a practice that drives every decision I make, from how I manage land to how I raise my children. That’s why my family is considering purchasing a property in **Hudson Valley**, NY, as a potential showcase for 5th World’s regenerative principles. It would allow me to truly live the values I espouse, and I would pour my heart and soul into creating a regenerative living masterpiece that embodies everything 5th World stands for.

To work with 5th World would be to fulfill a lifelong dream—a chance to contribute to the continuation of life on this planet, ensuring that future generations inherit a world rich in resources, health, and abundance. I’m driven by the belief that we can create a world where everyone thrives, where the synergy between technology and nature restores balance and ensures resilience.

Thank you for considering my application. I am eager to further discuss how my vision and experience can contribute to 5th World’s goals and how together, we can inspire a regenerative revolution.

Sincerely,  
**George Steward**  
Founder, Soil Grower

---

**1. Could you share with us how your experience will help you succeed in this role?**

My career has been built on merging two passions: technology and nature. Over the years, I’ve developed a deep understanding of the critical intersection between regenerative systems and modern technology. Through my work at **Soil Grower**, I’ve orchestrated partnerships that integrate AI, remote sensing, and ecological principles, providing solutions to enhance biodiversity and soil regeneration. This hands-on experience will allow me to bring practical, actionable insights to 5th World’s mission of driving land and property design toward sustainability and resilience.

In addition, my **ServiceNow** and **U.S. Army** experience has honed my project management skills. I’ve led teams to ensure mission-critical IT systems remained operational during high-stakes operations, a skill set that seamlessly transfers to managing complex regenerative projects. I’m excited to apply my leadership, data analysis, and environmental expertise to ensure the success of 5th World’s initiatives, delivering results that are both sustainable and scalable.

---

**2. Can you provide an example of a project where you successfully implemented regenerative systems or sustainable practices for a client? What were the key challenges, and how did you address them?**

One notable project involved regenerating land on a personal property in Texas, where I integrated **Earth Power Lodge** principles to develop sustainable animal shelters and enhance biodiversity. I designed these structures in harmony with natural cycles, aligning them with the sun’s path to maximize energy efficiency while ensuring that native and non-native plants provided both shade and food for the animals. This project improved overall land health, increasing water retention and nutrient uptake through natural soil amendments.

The key challenge was balancing the needs of livestock with maintaining a thriving ecosystem. By using regenerative biostimulants produced through my partnerships with **REGENiTECH**, I was able to boost plant health and create a balanced ecosystem. This project highlighted the importance of considering every organism in a system and tailoring interventions to achieve long-term stability.

---

**3. How do you approach client engagement and relationship management in consulting? Can you share an instance where you built a strong relationship with a client and how it impacted the project&#x27;s success?**

Client relationships are built on trust, active listening, and understanding their unique needs. My approach is to first deeply understand their objectives and challenges, then tailor solutions that align with their vision. During my tenure with **ServiceNow**, I spearheaded a **Proof of Concept (POC)** project for a high-profile client in the energy sector. The relationship grew through regular check-ins, ensuring I was accessible and responsive to their concerns.

By customizing workflows and reports to meet their specific needs, the client felt heard and valued, which not only increased their satisfaction but also led to a 25% boost in adoption rates. This engagement reinforced the importance of open communication and flexibility in meeting client demands while delivering solutions that have measurable impact.

---

**4. Describe a time when you had to manage multiple aspects of a consulting project, including timelines, budgets, and resources. How did you ensure that the project stayed on track and met client expectations?**

While transitioning the **7th Special Forces Group** from North Carolina to Florida, I was tasked with managing the relocation of IT infrastructure while ensuring operational continuity. This involved coordinating between multiple teams, managing a $695K budget, and adhering to strict timelines. I broke the project down into key phases, setting up regular status meetings to address any emerging issues before they became roadblocks.

To ensure we stayed on track, I leveraged project management tools and maintained detailed timelines, adjusting them when necessary. The result was a seamless transition, with 99.9% system uptime throughout the relocation. The key takeaway here was the importance of proactive communication, early identification of risks, and adaptability, ensuring that client and team expectations were met consistently.

---

**5. What methods or tools do you use for conducting detailed analyses and developing actionable recommendations? Can you give an example of how your analysis led to a successful outcome for a client?**

I use a combination of **GIS tools, data analytics platforms, and remote sensing technologies** to gather comprehensive data, analyze trends, and offer actionable insights. For example, in a land survey conducted in Arizona, I used remote sensing tools to assess soil health and water retention capabilities. By mapping the land’s topography and identifying areas of erosion, I developed a regenerative land management plan that included strategic placement of earthworks and planting of drought-resistant native species.

The result was improved soil stability and water retention, reducing erosion by 30%. By leveraging these tools and technologies, I was able to provide data-backed recommendations that the landowner could easily implement to achieve measurable results.

---

**6. How do you stay current with industry trends and best practices in land and property design, particularly in regenerative agriculture and ecosystem restoration? Can you provide an example of how you applied new knowledge to a recent project?**

Staying current in regenerative systems requires a commitment to continuous learning. I regularly engage with thought leaders and attend webinars on **agroforestry, permaculture, and biomimicry**. Most recently, I completed a course in **Water Science and Environmental Ethics**, which deepened my understanding of advanced water management systems. I applied this knowledge during a personal project where I integrated a rainwater harvesting system with natural swales and berms to improve water retention on a degraded plot of land.

The result was an increase in soil moisture levels by 20%, which enhanced plant growth and biodiversity. This example demonstrates how new knowledge can be directly applied to enhance the sustainability of a project and achieve tangible ecological benefits.

**USER**:
what are some data analytics platforms used in regenerative agriculture and living?

---

**ASSISTANT**:
In regenerative agriculture and living, data analytics platforms play a crucial role in monitoring, optimizing, and sustaining environmental systems. Here are some key platforms used in this field:

### 1. **FarmOS**
   - **Purpose**: Open-source farm management, planning, and record-keeping platform.
   - **Application**: Enables farmers to track field activities, inputs, and outputs with a focus on sustainability and regenerative practices. It integrates with IoT sensors and satellite data to monitor soil health, crop growth, and carbon sequestration.
   - **Key Features**: Customizable for specific farming practices, integrates geospatial data, and focuses on carbon footprint reduction.

### 2. **Granular**
   - **Purpose**: Farm management software for large-scale and small-scale farms.
   - **Application**: Offers analytics on crop performance, field data, and operational costs. Granular helps farmers optimize resources, improve yields, and incorporate regenerative practices by tracking soil health and water use.
   - **Key Features**: Provides financial planning, real-time data on field conditions, and analytics for decision-making in sustainable agriculture.

### 3. **Planet Labs**
   - **Purpose**: Satellite imagery and data platform.
   - **Application**: In regenerative agriculture, Planet Labs provides high-resolution imagery that helps monitor land use, soil health, crop development, and water management.
   - **Key Features**: Daily satellite images to track changes, evaluate the impact of regenerative practices, and assist in land restoration projects.

### 4. **Climate FieldView**
   - **Purpose**: Data collection and visualization for precision farming.
   - **Application**: Enables farmers to collect real-time data on crop health, field conditions, and soil moisture. Climate FieldView supports regenerative efforts by identifying trends in soil health and nutrient use efficiency.
   - **Key Features**: Visualization of yield maps, soil analysis, and variable-rate application tools.

### 5. **Regrow**
   - **Purpose**: Regenerative agriculture platform for tracking sustainability metrics.
   - **Application**: Uses satellite data, soil sampling, and advanced analytics to monitor soil carbon levels, biodiversity, and water use in regenerative agriculture systems.
   - **Key Features**: Tracks greenhouse gas emissions, verifies sustainability claims, and supports soil health programs.

### 6. **CIBO Technologies**
   - **Purpose**: Regenerative agriculture insights platform.
   - **Application**: Provides analytics on land use, soil health, and carbon credits. CIBO is used to predict the environmental and financial benefits of implementing regenerative practices.
   - **Key Features**: Carbon tracking, soil health monitoring, and economic impact analysis of regenerative practices.

### 7. **FarmLogs**
   - **Purpose**: Farm management software focused on sustainability.
   - **Application**: Offers insights into weather patterns, soil conditions, and field performance to help optimize regenerative agricultural practices.
   - **Key Features**: Automated tracking of inputs, yield analytics, and crop health monitoring.

These platforms are essential in regenerative agriculture for optimizing resource use, improving soil health, reducing carbon footprints, and ensuring that regenerative practices are profitable and sustainable.

**ASSISTANT**:
I utilize a diverse set of GIS tools, data analytics platforms, and remote sensing technologies to gather comprehensive data, analyze trends, and provide actionable insights. Tools like **FarmOS** and **SkyFi Analytics** allow me to collect and visualize geospatial data on land use, crop health, and soil conditions, offering real-time feedback on key metrics such as soil moisture and carbon sequestration. Combined with **BadElf** GPS receivers for precision mapping and **weather stations** to monitor microclimatic conditions, I am able to paint a complete picture of an area’s health.

In a recent land survey in Arizona, I applied these technologies to assess soil health and water retention. Using **SkyFi satellite imagery** and **FarmOS**, I mapped the land’s topography, identified erosion-prone areas, and tracked real-time changes in vegetation. By incorporating **soil health sensors**—capable of measuring organic matter, moisture, and compaction levels—I could directly assess how these factors influenced plant growth and water absorption. Furthermore, I used **remote sensing tools** for tree health analysis, measuring leaf chlorophyll and water stress levels to gauge the vitality of various species.

These insights were invaluable in crafting a regenerative land management plan that involved earthworks for improved water retention and the planting of drought-tolerant native species. As a result, the soil’s stability increased, and water retention improved significantly, reducing erosion by 30%. These data-backed strategies ensured that the landowner could not only implement the recommendations effectively but also track progress and measure outcomes using the same technologies.

**ASSISTANT**:
I utilize a blend of advanced tools and hands-on techniques to gather detailed data for land and soil health assessments. For instance, in a project in Georgetown, TX, I used the **Microbiometer** to measure the bacterial-to-fungal ratio, which allowed me to quickly assess the biological health of the soil without needing to send samples to a lab. When more sophisticated sensors weren’t available, I relied on manual tools like a **soil compaction tool** to gauge soil density and assess its ability to support plant growth.

During this project, I combined these techniques with **GIS mapping** and **remote sensing tools** to develop a comprehensive regenerative land management plan. This included strategic earthworks to improve water retention and the introduction of native species to enhance biodiversity. These data-driven decisions resulted in healthier soil, reduced erosion, and better water retention—factors critical to the success of the project.

Davey Resource Group, Inc., is a leader in the natural resource, environmental, and forestry consulting industries throughout the United States.  The Davey Tree Expert Company provides research-driven tree services, grounds maintenance and environmental consulting for residential, utility, commercial and environmental partners in the U.S. and Canada. We care about our clients, each other and the world around us. We offer the resources, size and stability of a big company while maintaining the culture, entrepreneurial spirit and feel of a small one. We invest in our employees by offering industry-leading training, technology and benefits that lead to a rewarding and safe work experience at all levels. Wherever you want to grow your career, there’s a place for you at Davey. To learn more, visit Davey.com.

Beyond my technical abilities, I believe that my approach to sustainability and environmental stewardship aligns with DRG&#x27;s values of safety, integrity, and leadership. I am committed to expanding my expertise in utility vegetation management and would be honored to contribute to the continued success of DRG while advancing my career in the green industry.

Sincerely,  
George Steward

Position Title: Field Sales Manager

Reports to: Director of Sales – National  

Start Date: Q4 2024

Location: Central, TX 

Company Profile:
Force of Nature is a champion for regenerative agriculture and wildlife conservation.  We are committed to educating consumers that animal agriculture, when managed in a manner that emulates the diverse harmony in nature, improves welfare, creates the most nutrient dense food available and ultimately produces a positive return on the planet. We exist to give consumers an opportunity to vote for environmental regeneration through their purchasing power of fresh/frozen meat and to ultimately reclaim the legacy of meat. At a time when industrialized and commoditized conventional agriculture is wreaking devastation and many false profits are generating headlines with lab based or highly processed alternatives that are really no better for you or the environment; we are here to prove that nature got it right. There is no doubt that together, we can heal our environment, restore our health, and end the agricultural system that is depleting our natural resources.

Position Scope:
Field Sales Manager role will work cross functionally in the development and execution of field sales and marketing related programs at the retailer level and on projects ranging from sales support to marketing support and execution.

Major Responsibilities:
*Note that responsibilities may be added or adjusted over time.

Field Sales
Lead field sales efforts.
Build and execute strategic market blitz plans to support sales in regions &amp; retailers that are critical to sales department goals and objectives (2-3 market blitzes per month).
Deliver follow up from field sales blitzes in timely and accurate manner effectively delivering positive return on the investment of time and company resources in the field
Work with Director of Sales and Regional Sales Managers to help map out quarterly field sales plans and goals
Track progress on field sales blitzes and maintain comprehensive log to help RSMs channel communication to retail buyers and category managers
Represent the brand to the highest Force of Nature standard in the field
Create target list of independents and call on potential customers while on field sales blitzes to gain distribution into new accounts
Accountability to annual sales plan
Ownership and communication of recurring updates to plans and forecasts within assigned accounts. Support in measuring performance against expectations
Support in building and supporting of annual trade promotional calendar.
Identify and execute on opportunities to expand the sales of FON across all channels, which includes working with broker and distributor networks to maximize sales and distribution opportunities
Ensure timely execution on new item introductions, schematic implementation and promotional programming and that they have all necessary resources required to succeed in the market (e.g., product samples, sell sheets, promotional calendars, etc)
Ensure that all POS &amp; Swag (e.g. freezers, shelf talkers, trays, hats, t-shirts, VIP Coupons etc.) is utilized effectively in the marketplace.
Analyze distribution reports to determine market coverage and opportunities
Conduct in-store audits (via broker management or in person) to ensure merchandising standards are adhered to and promotional programming is executed
Identify opportunities to build strong connections with key individuals and form meaningful and impactful relationships that benefit the FON brand (from consumer to buyers and everyone in between).
Support in executing FoN goals in multiple selling channels: 
Retail
Support sales in key independent, regional &amp; national retailers executing market sales blitzes routinely and with great results
Support distributor sales efforts driving increased ACV &amp; velocity at the shelf
Food Service
Work with Foodservice manager to support growth in this channel, especially in the local market
Support sales efforts at regional foodservice distributor partners
Direct Wholesale
Identify and sell into key non-traditional sales outlets
Support the development of and execution of innovative selling opportunities
Support in onboarding new retailers, distributors and brokers in vetting, gathering and completing of essential onboarding documents.
Technical capabilities for using suite of systems to support sales planning, customer management, analytics
Marketing
Aid in retailer marketing support execution driving maximum value out of opportunities including the execution and implementation of POS, signage, merchandising, demo support and distribution of swag.
Execute strategic &quot;demos&quot; (educational and serving food) at retail locations and events as needed
Assist/lead the execution of trade shows &amp; events as assigned
Assist in the project management of internal projects and 3rd party POS, printing and merchandising contractor timelines and deliverables that support sales.
Cross Functional Support
Cultural support both internally and externally (ensuring things like handwritten notes to top key accounts, notes to new buyers at launch, influencer follow-up execution with samples) are executed
Support any needs of the business and be a trusted and dedicated member of the team.
Work closely with Sales &amp; Operations to ensure accountability to forecasts

Team player

Dear Force of Nature Team,

I’m writing with immense excitement to apply for the **Field Sales Manager** role at **Force of Nature**. Your mission to reclaim the legacy of meat and champion **regenerative agriculture** directly aligns with my own life’s work and passions. As someone who has personally benefited from **Force of Nature&#x27;s** products—especially since my son with **FPIES** relies on **bison** as his primary source of nutrition—I feel a deep connection to your brand and its values.

Throughout my career, I’ve blended my expertise in technology with my passion for **ecological restoration**. From serving in the **U.S. Army** to launching my own **plant healthcare business**, I’ve cultivated a unique ability to merge **cutting-edge tools** with **ancient wisdom** like **biomimicry** and **Traditional Ecological Knowledge (TEK)**. Through **Soil Grower**, I’ve pioneered **regenerative agriculture practices** on personal and community projects, using **biostimulants** to increase biodiversity by over 30% and improve soil health.

What excites me about the **Field Sales Manager** role is the chance to connect with communities and retailers, expanding the reach of **Force of Nature** and promoting food systems that heal the planet. I envision a future where **biomimicry**, **biodynamic practices**, and **regenerative systems** drive not just **sustainability**, but **abundance**. In particular, I would love to see us collaborate on initiatives like a **Soil Grower nonprofit**, showcasing **pioneering techniques in soil regeneration**, with **bison as the original soil builders**.

When I spoke with Clint about the **East Regional Sales Manager** role last year, the only challenge was the extensive travel while raising a newborn. My son is now 1, and I’m ready to dive fully into a role where I can **champion regenerative agriculture** and support Force of Nature’s growth. My sales background in industries as diverse as **enterprise software, luxury goods, and plant healthcare** gives me the flexibility to **adapt to diverse customer needs** while remaining focused on long-term relationships.

I am beyond passionate about this work, and I will **pour my heart and soul** into making **Force of Nature** not just a leading regenerative brand but a **catalyst for global change**. I am confident that my experience, combined with my personal connection to your products, will make me a valuable asset to your team.

Thank you for considering my application. I look forward to the opportunity to discuss how I can contribute to **Force of Nature’s** success and help take regenerative agriculture to the next level.

Sincerely,  
**George Steward**

With a passionately autodidactic, immersive, and enduring education in technology, ecological and human resiliency, and nature relatedness combined with a broadly distributed history as a soldier, technician, natural solutions consultant, and sales professional, I offer…

BLUF: I have a burning desire to contribute significantly to planetary+humanitarian health using a biological/nature-first approach. This fervent purpose-driven mission stems from an unwavering necessity to leave the world better than I found it. It also comes from uncovering unknown unknowns through deep introspection and incessantly seeking my truth. I am innately qualified to connect austere elements of function, design, and human understanding. I am eager to help restore regenerative principles on every level from the structure of soil to the composition of molecules in the sky. My last role involved five months of hands-on training as a Solution Consultant. This is where I honed my skills in storytelling, value selling, customer success, presentation, and martech that I had previously developed through various sales roles and entrepreneurial ventures. I exist to continue the fight for symbiosis between human and nature.

HOMETOWN: Monroeville, AL 

TOP 3 MEATS: beef heart+beaver tail, bison tripe, beef liver

FAVORITE WILDLIFE: Honey Buzzard

WHAT ARE YOU GRATEFUL FOR?: My family, my purpose. The instinct to know that my being whole required a regeneration cycle in order to become my best for them and for you. The unshakable knowing that we are intrinsically and inseparably connected to nature. The enduring opportunity to be a force multiplier of positive global change through consumer support of regenerative agriculture. The wisdom in the philosophy that we are what we eat.

WHY REGENERATIVE? Biomimicry is the sincerest form of flattery in nature. To live is to let live. Cooperation is the process of continual evolution resulting in stronger communities. To be regenerative is to be masterfully adaptable keepers of the water and wholesome stewards of the land that we share space upon this earth with all other life forms. To live is to be truly like the water in which gives us life. To experience resiliency as a process rather than simply a result requires grit in the responsibility of tending our gardens and our guts with the same fervor. To command the best from our grocers, our walk must be in harmony with our talk.

I have implemented strategies in my personal journey that directly relate to the Force of Nature core mission of restoring regenerative principles. I am poised to build on that foundation and use my skills for good where it matters most. I am prepared to extend the ideals of regeneration, transformation, and symbiotic resiliency to communities by being a servant leader. I have a proven record of excellent customer service, records management, data analysis, business development, and producing quality results. My top five Clifton strengths are ideation, learner, intellection, responsibility, and command which means I have an inherent growth mindset and a duty to share knowledge for the benefit of all life.

My qualifications include:

14 years of military experience, 6 in Special Operations
12 years of IT project management including interstate organizational moves
4 years of consultative sales experience spanning many industries
Advanced education in records management and office systems technology 
Excellent writing, editing, speaking, and presentation skills
Strong understanding of evaluation, assessment, and reporting
Planning and Operations skills developed through education and experience

I look forward to working directly with Joe and Pete to drive growth results in the East. Dear **Clint Clancy** and **Force of Nature Team**,  

I am thrilled to apply for the **Field Sales Manager** position with **Force of Nature**. This role isn’t just about selling products—it’s about contributing to a mission that is central to my life and personal values. I am here for that mission.

**My Personal Journey with Force of Nature:** As a loyal customer, Force of Nature products have been vital in my family&#x27;s life—especially for my son, who has **FPIES** and relies heavily on your **bison products** as his primary source of nutrition. I know firsthand the power of regenerative meat, and that connection fuels my desire to help spread your message far and wide. In many ways, your products have been as crucial to my family as they are to the land they come from. This personal experience gives me a unique perspective and drive to **advocate for Force of Nature&#x27;s impact** on the lives of consumers and the planet.

**My Professional Journey:** My career has spanned over a decade in high-stakes environments—from leading **IT projects in Special Operations** to launching my own company, **Soil Grower**, where I apply **biomimicry** and **Traditional Ecological Knowledge (TEK)** to create regenerative systems. I am finishing my **Environmental Science degree**, further deepening my knowledge to drive impactful solutions in the green industry. Starting my **plant healthcare business**, I have been actively involved in **soil regeneration projects**, utilizing **biostimulants** to increase biodiversity and improve soil health. Every piece of my background has equipped me to dive into this role with expertise and passion.

**My Vision with Force of Nature:** As a **Field Sales Manager**, I am ready to do more than sell. I’m here to be an **ambassador for your mission**, helping to create long-term, meaningful connections with consumers and partners. I see the opportunity to further expand **Force of Nature’s** footprint by partnering with key players in **sustainability**, **biodynamic farming**, and **soil regeneration**. I envision expanding the narrative by launching a nonprofit arm through **Soil Grower**, where we showcase the **true soil builders**—bison, fauna, flora—and the **keystone species** that make regenerative agriculture possible. Together, we can build thriving ecosystems that not only regenerate soil but uplift entire communities.

**My Unique Qualifications:**
- **14 years of military experience**, including **6 in Special Operations**, where I honed leadership, strategic planning, and resilience in high-pressure environments.
- **Consultative sales expertise**, with hands-on experience launching new businesses and creating solutions that balance **people, planet, and profit**.
- A personal connection to Force of Nature’s **mission**, driving me to become an active force for change and a true partner to every customer and retailer I interact with.
- **Technical expertise** in using data-driven platforms like **GIS**, **remote sensing tools**, and **biostimulants** to drive soil regeneration—knowledge that translates to understanding what makes your products so essential for our environment.

**Why This Role Fits:** While my interview with Clint last year for the **East Regional Sales Manager** role was positive, at the time, I couldn’t commit to the heavy travel requirements due to my newborn son. Now that he’s a year old, I am ready to fully dedicate myself to this mission. This role aligns perfectly with my background, passions, and desire to work **hands-on in the field**, applying my skills to **drive growth** and **create impact** from **soil to stomach**.

**Excited to Join the Team:** I am particularly looking forward to collaborating with **Joe, Pete, Marshall, and the entire sales team** to craft field strategies that meet and exceed goals. I’m eager to work closely with **Renee and Emily** on **brand-building** and messaging, contributing innovative ideas that expand your impact. Finally, I can’t wait to join **Walker on the ranch**, experiencing firsthand how **Force of Nature&#x27;s regenerative systems** function in the field—and being part of a **wildly successful** team that is revolutionizing the way we think about meat and sustainability.

I am eager to bring my **passion**, **experience**, and **dedication** to the Force of Nature team. I am ready to contribute to the **global regenerative movement** and to help you drive measurable, meaningful change. I would be honored to discuss how my background and vision align with **Force of Nature’s** goals. Please feel free to contact me at (737) 234-0110 or george@soilgrower.org to discuss further.

Thank you for considering my application. I am beyond excited for the opportunity to help build a **future where humans and nature thrive together**.

Sincerely,  
**George Steward**

**October 14th, 2024**

**Force of Nature Team**
