Dear Clint Clancy and Force of Nature Team,  

I am excited to apply for the Field Sales Manager position at Force of Nature. This is not just another career opportunity for me—it is a calling that aligns with my passion for regenerative agriculture, biodiversity, and building thriving communities. I view this role not merely as a sales job, but as a mission-driven opportunity to be part of the transformative work Force of Nature is leading, and I am eager to contribute wholeheartedly.  

**My Personal Journey with Force of Nature:**  
As a loyal customer, Force of Nature has played a critical role in my family’s life—particularly for my son, who has an FPIES chicken allergy and relies heavily on your bison products as his primary source of nutrition. I have witnessed firsthand the value of regenerative meat, and this personal connection inspires my desire to amplify your message and expand your impact. Force of Nature’s products have been essential to my family’s health, and this experience gives me a deep, authentic drive to advocate for your mission of restoring ecosystems and transforming food systems.  

**My Professional Journey:**  
Over the last decade, I’ve transitioned from leading high-stakes IT projects in Special Operations to launching my own company, Soil Grower, where I apply biomimicry, Traditional Ecological Knowledge (TEK), and natural intelligence to create regenerative systems. I am currently completing my Environmental Science degree, which deepens my understanding of ecosystem resilience and land regeneration. Through Soil Grower, I’ve worked on soil health and biodiversity projects, developing solutions that enhance ecosystems and empower communities. These experiences have prepared me to dive into this role with the passion and expertise necessary to help drive Force of Nature’s mission forward.

**My Vision with Force of Nature:**  
In this role, I see myself not just as a sales manager but as an ambassador for your regenerative movement. I am passionate about building long-term relationships with consumers, retailers, and sustainability partners to further expand your impact. I also envision expanding Force of Nature’s narrative through initiatives like launching a nonprofit under Soil Grower, which would spotlight the true soil builders—bison and other keystone species—who are at the heart of regenerative agriculture. Together, we can showcase how these animals and practices create thriving ecosystems that uplift both the land and the communities connected to it.

**My Unique Qualifications:**  
- **14 years of military experience**, including 6 in Special Operations, developing leadership, strategic planning, and resilience in high-pressure environments.
- **Consultative sales expertise**: Launching new businesses and implementing regenerative solutions that balance people, planet, and profit.
- **Technical expertise**: In using data-driven platforms and understanding how natural systems interconnect with business strategies, skills critical to advocating for Force of Nature’s environmental mission.
- **Personal connection**: To Force of Nature’s regenerative principles, driving my commitment to advocating for your impact on consumers and the planet.

**Why This Role Fits Now:**  
During my previous interview with Clint for the East Regional Sales Manager position, I couldn’t commit to the heavy travel required due to my newborn son. Now that he’s a year old, I am fully ready to dedicate myself to this mission. This role aligns perfectly with my skills and passions, allowing me to actively contribute on the ground, helping to grow the Force of Nature brand from soil to stomach.

**Excited to Join the Team:**  
I am eager to collaborate with the sales and marketing teams to craft impactful strategies that exceed goals while building brand resonance. I look forward to working directly with the team on the ranch, gaining firsthand experience with Force of Nature’s regenerative systems and bringing that knowledge into the field. Together, we can continue revolutionizing the way the world understands meat and regeneration.

I would be honored to discuss how my background, passion, and vision align with Force of Nature’s mission. You can reach me at (737) 234-0110 or george@soilgrower.org. Thank you for considering my application. I am thrilled for the opportunity to contribute to a future where humans and nature thrive together.

Sincerely,  
George Steward  
Founder, Soil Grower

Job Description
Team

Come join the AI Solution Success team in the Advanced Technology Group (ATG). We are focused on customer-facing and internal projects. You’ll work alongside a team of seasoned professionals working on leading edge, innovative projects to help drive the business. This global team is highly collaborative and shares the best practices. We work on scalable AI (Artificial Intelligence) solutions, so if you are a results-oriented visionary that likes to dream big, come join our team!

Who we are?

We are a team composed of cross-functional SMEs from ATG, Platform, Business Units, Customer Outcomes and QE and multiple customer-focused teams of ML, SW, and QE engineers that bring varied perspectives and diverse expertise to drive customer adoption of AI experiences, as well as guide customer driven innovation within ATG.

What&#x27;s our purpose?

Accelerate value realization of AI-powered workflows by customers at scale.

What we do?

Work with early adopters to validate AI solutions and realize value by learning and quickly improving the solution on real customer data. We&#x27;ll create practical playbooks to guide new implementations, boost adoption and drive future product innovation. Some of the work the team has been instrumental at is to improve customer adoption of our multi-language Natural Language Understanding (NLU), AI search, Issue Auto-Resolution and other related AI solutions with customers.

What you get to do in this role:

The AI Solution Manager is responsible for defining, planning &amp; leading programs for the implementation of AI solutions for our customers to solve complex business challenges. This role requires a good understanding of AI and machine learning, as well as the ability to work effectively with cross-functional teams to deliver solutions that meet the needs of our customers. The AI Solution Manager will also be responsible for managing customer relationships and engagements during the program lifecycle, ensuring that our customers are satisfied with our solutions and that they are getting the most out of their AI investments while at the same time ensuring learnings are captured for product improvement.

The AI Solution Manager is responsible for overseeing the successful delivery of the defined solution to meet the customer&#x27;s requirements within budget and on time, following ServiceNow&#x27;s NowCreate methodology, and collaborating with the customer project team and partners. The AI Solution Manager ensures proper governance and support from team members, addressing risks and issues. They assemble and lead the ServiceNow resources, track progress, and manage any deviations.

Key responsibilities include:

Leading the delivery team, managing engagement governance, timeline, scope, risk, change management, resourcing, reporting, and financials. The AI Solution Manager also manages the business relationship with customers, providing regular updates to both customers and internal executive teams. They work with cross-functional projects, senior-level executives, and customers to deliver a unique customer experience.
The AI Solution Manager acts as a thought leader, guiding successful delivery and customer outcomes. They facilitate collaboration, decision-making, and customer buy-in for proposed solutions. Coaching and managing team members to enable achievement of engagement deliverables and desired business outcomes.
The AI Solution Manager manages multiple programs simultaneously, identifies gaps, proposes solutions, presents the value proposition to customers during and after the initiative, and actively facilitates capture of the best practices and learnings from both the customer and the internal project team

2. **Managing customer relationships**:
   - Your experience in **consultative sales** (e.g., launching Soil Grower and consulting with property owners and developers) has refined your ability to build long-lasting customer relationships. This ties well with ServiceNow&#x27;s need for someone who can manage and nurture relationships with **strategic customers**.

3. **Capturing feedback and improving solutions**:
   - Your background in **data-driven decision making** and **GIS tools** to assess land and environmental projects, paired with your **ServiceNow consulting role**, highlights your ability to gather client feedback, identify gaps, and optimize solutions for better results—skills required to lead customer-centric AI projects.

### **Relevant Experience**:
1. **Project Management &amp; Cross-Functional Leadership**:
   - Managed complex IT projects during military service, overseeing multiple elements like **budget, teams, and strategic goals**.
   - Led 50+ Proof of Concept engagements at ServiceNow, managing cross-functional teams to deliver innovative AI and software solutions.

2. **AI and Data Analytics**:
   - Experience with **AI tools** and **data analytics platforms** like FarmOS, SkyFi, and GIS for environmental assessments and project optimization in your own company translates to understanding the analytical backbone of AI solutions in ServiceNow&#x27;s platform.
   
3. **Customer-Focused Solutions**:
   - Your focus on **customer outcomes** in sales roles, where you delivered actionable results using technology for environmental health, shows your alignment with ServiceNow’s mission to deliver **customer-focused AI solutions** and boost adoption. Your role at ServiceNow as a **Solution Consultant** showcases your ability to engage directly with clients and deliver technology solutions that meet business needs.

4. **Business Relationship &amp; Engagement**:
   - As a **Founder at Soil Grower**, you built partnerships and implemented **ecosystem-enhancing technologies**, directly correlating with **building business relationships** and enhancing client experiences. You have **interpersonal skills** and a client-focused approach essential for this role.

### **Desired Qualifications**:
1. **Project Management Skills**:
